Sun Dianying's Telegram Reply to Pang Bingxun and Others

Requests Sending of Personnel, Claims to Have Resigned and No Longer Involves Himself with the Troops

Situation in Ningyuan Unclear

Internal Disintegration of Sun's Army

Military Expenses for Jin Army Not Yet Agreed Upon

(Beiping) Pang Bingxun, Hu Yukun, Ji Yiqiao, jointly telegraphed Sun Dianying a few days ago, urging him to leave the army. Sun recently replied (on the 23rd). Pang and others went to He Yingqin at Jurentang at 6 p.m. on the 25th, in addition to presenting Sun's reply telegram for review, the aftermath of Sun's troops and whether to send personnel were also discussed in detail. Sun's telegram is as follows: The telegram of the 19th has been respectfully received, and I am grateful for your protection. I am able to follow the wishes of my three elder brothers, and I believe you can trust me. I deeply believe that you can decide my proposition. If you can send someone to come, I will listen to everything. Even if you send a soldier to order me to go to Beiping, I will definitely be able to go with him. As long as you do not abandon me and give me your attention, I will be extremely grateful. I have resigned from the troops and will no longer be involved. I respectfully reply to you, hoping for your consideration. Your brother, Sun Kuiyuan, kowtows. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

(Beiping) According to sources, Sun's army is facing enemies on three sides, and its rear route has been cut off. Lu Fengnian's troops in Dengkou are showing signs of retreating to Shizuizi. There are reports that Zhuan Sunziyu's brigade is preparing to revolt. Internal disintegration within Sun's army is apparent. However, Sun is still secretly colluding with the Red bandits of Sichuan and Shaanxi, plotting to harm the Northwest. The authorities have decided to implement both pacification and suppression measures for the military affairs of suppressing Sun, to facilitate easier results. The issue of military expenses for the Fu army has not been agreed upon, and there is still no definite date for returning to Suiyuan. The claim of Jin-Sui armies following and pursuing is only publicly stated by the Jin side, and the authorities have not yet received a report. Regarding the battle situation in Ningyuan, the truth is unclear because there has been no telegram from Ma for a week. Some claim that a portion of Sun's army has crossed Ningxia and fled south, but the location is unknown. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Beiping) Since the Jin-Sui armies departed from western Suiyuan, the vanguard is now only ten miles away from Sansheng Palace, and the rear units are also advancing successively. Sun's army is very panicked because it has lost contact with both the front and rear. They have been fleeing in panic for days, preparing to retreat to Dengkou Shizuizi, but many have been intercepted and disarmed by Wang Jingguo's troops. The morale of the army is dissipated, and it has shown signs of disintegration. The enemy on the western route recently attacked Pingluo in Ningxia again, but failed each time. Now, feeling threatened by the northern route, they have stopped attacking. The fighting near Ningyuan has gradually eased. The rumor that Sun's troops bypassed and pursued Ningbian in an attempt to flee into Gansu is not necessarily reliable. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

(Nanjing) The chairman of Gansu Province, Zhu Shaoliang, replied to the province's office in Nanjing on the 24th, stating that the enemy and our troops are still in stalemate north of Ningyuan, and rumors are not to be believed. Xu's bandits and Sun are too far apart and difficult to merge. Special reply. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Nanjing) The Peiping Military Sub-Council telegraphed Nanjing, stating that Sun Dianying has no remorse and determination to repent and is still preparing for war. In addition to ordering the armies of Gansu, Ningxia, and Qinghai to defend against attacks, most of the Jin-Sui armies have crossed Dengkou, and the vanguard troops have already contacted Sun's army. Currently, Sun, seeing that he is surrounded on all sides, is personally commanding and supervising the attack on Ningyuan on the front line, in order to flee towards Lingwu Zhongwei area. The military council has decided to tighten the alert on that army. (Special dispatch, 25th)

Japanese Planes Transporting Ammunition, Storing a Large Quantity in Duolun

(Beiping) A telegram from Zhangjiakou states that several Japanese planes are transporting ammunition from Rehe to Guyuan Second and Fourth Districts and Duolun. Duolun is already full of more than ten houses. Their intention is known. (Special dispatch, 25th)

A War in Kangzang Seems Inevitable

(Nanjing) An official of the Mongolian Association said that the Kangzang dispute has not yet been resolved. A few days ago, the Tibetan bandits, because their request for Liu Wenhui to cede Ganzhan and other places was not granted, are dispatching troops and have gathered on the front line, totaling about 30,000 to 40,000 people. Now Liu Wenhui is also waiting in strict formation, and it is expected that war may be difficult to avoid. (Special dispatch, 25th)

Shenyang Explosives Factory Explosion

(Tianjin) The explosives manufacturing plant of the Shenyang Arsenal suddenly exploded a few days ago while manufacturing explosives for blank cartridges, killing one Japanese worker and seriously injuring two Chinese workers. Two Chinese workers were slightly injured. The cause of the explosion is under investigation. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

Eastern Guizhou Allied Army Reorganized by Wang Jialie

(Changsha) The three units of the Eastern Guizhou Allied Army, Che Mingyi, Lei Mingjiu, and Yang Qichang, have all been reorganized by Wang Jialie and placed under the command of Bai Huizhang, moving and stationing in Sixian for reorganization and training. (Special dispatch, 25th)

Xiao Kong Bandit Gang Flees South

(Changsha) The Xiao Gao bandit troops crossed the river from Zhelin and fled south. Liu Yinggu has deployed forces to intercept and suppress them. (Special dispatch, 25th)

Righteous Army Attacks Jiamusi

Japanese Immigrant Instructor Seriously Wounded

(Changchun) According to the Kwantung Army, at 1 a.m. on the 16th of this month, more than a hundred members of the Righteous Army attacked the headquarters of the Japanese Armed Immigrant Group in Yongfeng Town, Jiamusi. After a fierce battle, the immigrant instructor Sato and military doctor Terazaki were seriously wounded. Most of the houses where the immigrants lived were also burned down. The Righteous Army saw that their goal had been achieved and quickly retreated to their original defenses. The Immigrant Group was greatly panicked and fled one after another. (Delayed dispatch from the China United Press, 25th)

Japanese Ruffians Cause Trouble in Luan County

(Tianjin) Japanese ruffians in Luan County have organized a Japanese Language Research Support Association, using the slogan of Japanese-Manchu-Chinese ethnic friendship, recruiting local ruffians and rogues into the association. Each person pays a membership fee of one yuan. After joining the association, each household hangs a wooden plaque of the Japanese Language Research Support Association, and the war zone security team and police are not allowed to interfere with their actions. Members are equipped with bronze badges, enter and exit government offices, and run rampant in the city. When something happens, the Japanese come forward to protect them and openly interfere with the judiciary. The Luan County trial commissioner resigned in anger, and the area has fallen into chaos. (Special dispatch, 25th)

Ma Zhanshan Arrives in Beiping Secretly

(Beiping) After being assassinated in Tianjin, Ma Zhanshan came to Beiping by car on the 25th. His whereabouts are secret, and he has not met with many visitors. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Beiping) Ma Zhanshan arrived in Beiping on the 24th and is residing at Wan Fulin's residence. Reporters visited, but Wan's residence claimed he had not arrived. According to someone close to Ma, the person who came to Beiping yesterday was Lang Guanpu, who was in charge of discussing Ma's relocation to Beiping. Wan said that Beiping is easier to protect, so he hopes that Ma will move to Beiping. The reason for Ma's assassination is that a certain party was dissatisfied and provided a huge sum of more than 200,000 yuan to a group to mastermind the assassination. The group obtained the money and rented an empty room next to Ma's residence in the British Concession of Tianjin, planning to dig a wall into Ma's residence to carry out the assassination. The Public Security Bureau detected this and sent a secret agent to join the group. Therefore, on the day of the assassination, the perpetrators could not escape and may be tried by military law in the future. (Special dispatch, 25th)

Mongolian Association Urges Prince Yun to Stay

(Nanjing) The Mongolian Association believes that Prince Yun's leadership of Mongolian affairs is highly reputable and has telegraphed again to urge him to stay and continue his difficult task. (Special dispatch, 25th)

Zhang Xueliang Arrives in Hankou Yesterday Morning

Receiving Personnel in Batches

Will Report to the Headquarters Today

To Inspect Bandit Areas After Officially Assuming Office

(Hankou) Zhang Xueliang arrived in Hankou at 8:30 a.m. on the 25th aboard the Yongsui warship. Gao Lingbai, Tang Guozhen, Tan Hai, Shen Zutong, Wu Zhongxian, and a secretary and two adjutants came with him. He Chengjun, Qian Dajun, Zhang Qun, Xu Yuanquan, Ye Peng, and others were at the Sanbei Wharf to welcome him. The garrison brigade and the Minquan warship navy were responsible for guarding the lighter wharf. Zhang was in good spirits. After landing, he went to the Bank Association to meet with various dignitaries, and then went to the headquarters to report for duty. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Hankou) Zhang Xueliang received He Chengjun, Zhang Qun, Qian Dajun, Xu Yuanquan, Xia Douyin, and Ye Peng at the headquarters at noon on the 25th. He and Zhang respectively reported on the military and political situation. Then, he received Sun Lianzhong, Shangguan Yunxiang, Pei Changhui, and other generals, as well as provincial and municipal party committees in batches. He Zhuguo and Wei Hailou also rushed to see him to ask for instructions. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Hankou) He Zhuguo, upon Zhang's summons, arrived in Hankou at noon on the 25th, accompanied by Secretary Hu Shao. Hu said that He's troops were ordered to pursue and suppress the remnants of Liu Guitang's bandits. With the mission completed, they are being demobilized. Liu's bandits are currently fleeing to Lingbao and are being pursued and suppressed by Gao Guizi. He met Liu Zhi in Kaifeng and came to Hankou in response to the summons and will return to the north within days. Wei Hailou will stay in Henan and come to Hankou to see Zhang within days. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Hankou) Zhang Xueliang paid a return visit to He Chengjun and Ye Peng in the afternoon of the 25th. On the 26th, he crossed the river to visit Zhang Qun and went to the headquarters to report for duty. After officially assuming office on March 1, he will inspect the bandit areas. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Hankou) Zhang Xueliang told reporters that the date of assuming office has not been determined. He intends to first report for duty. The organization of the headquarters remains the same without any changes. He plans to inspect the bandit areas in the three provinces. As for the bandit suppression operations and troop movements, due to military secrets, he could not disclose them. Whether to go to Peiping or Jiangxi is not yet determined. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Hankou) He Chengjun has decided to continue his inspection tour. He said on the 25th that the date of departure will be determined after Zhang assumes office. If the weather is clear, he will first go to Anlu to attend the memorial service for the 26th Army. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Hankou) The bandit suppression generals of the three provinces, except for those who cannot leave their defense due to official business, are scheduled to come to Hankou within days to report on defense matters and request instructions. (Special dispatch, 25th)

Guangdong Generals Discuss Bandit Suppression

Chen Jitang Prepares to Welcome Chiang Ting-wen

Li Yangjing and Lin Yunguai to Inspect Eastern Guangdong

Southwest Political Council to Discuss Important Cases Today

(Hong Kong) Chen Jitang summoned Yu Hanmou, Li Yangjing, and others on the 25th to discuss bandit suppression. Yu is scheduled to return to Jiangxi on the 26th or 27th. Yang Dezhao, upon Chen's summons, is scheduled to return south in a day or two. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Hong Kong) Chiang Ting-wen is scheduled to fly from Fuzhou to Guangzhou on the 27th to meet with Chen Jitang and discuss bandit suppression plans. A central representative, Mr. Lin, will come with him. Chen Jitang has arranged the Tuisi Garden in preparation for welcoming them. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Hong Kong) The Political Council is scheduled to discuss the restructuring of the provincial government and the issue of Pu Yi's usurpation of the throne on the 26th, inviting senior military and political officials from various agencies to participate. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Hong Kong) The Guangdong students donated to purchase a plane, which was named Student on the 25th. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Hong Kong) Guangdong is scheduled to hold a memorial service for Wu Chaoshu on March 14. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Hong Kong) Li Yangjing and Lin Yunguai are scheduled to inspect eastern Guangdong on the 26th. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Hong Kong) Lin Yunguai is scheduled to depart from the province on the Guangzhou-Kowloon special train to Zhangmutou at noon on the 26th, then transfer to Huizhou, and proceed along the coast to Lufeng and then to Shantou, before going to Chaozhou and Meizhou to inspect. He has ordered the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway Bureau to prepare a car for his use. Li Yangjing will also travel with Lin back to Shantou to convene an East District Pacification Conference. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

(Hong Kong) Lin Yizhong is scheduled to inspect Wenchang and other counties on the 26th. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

(Hong Kong) Yu Hanmou is scheduled to leave the province on the 27th to return to Yu and preside over the bandit suppression military affairs. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

Chen Yi and Zhang Zhen Urge Chen Zhaoying to Go to Fujian

(Nanjing) Chen Yi and Zhang Zhen telegraphed Nanjing, urging Chen Zhaoying to go to Fujian. Chen is still in his hometown. According to news from his residence in Nanjing, he will not be able to return to Nanjing for several days. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Nanjing) Chen Ticheng, the director of the Fujian Construction Department, went to Shanghai on the 25th to meet with Song Ziwen to discuss the construction of Fujian Province. After completing the matters, he will return to Fujian. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Hangzhou) Chen Zhaoying is scheduled to leave his hometown of Pujiang after the first day of next month, stop briefly in Hangzhou, and then go to Nanjing to ask the central government for instructions before going to Fujian. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

Vietnamese Overseas Chinese Jointly Suggest to the Central Government

(Nanjing) Overseas Chinese residing in Vietnam, because overseas Chinese merchants are oppressed by heavy taxes before the signing of the new Sino-Vietnamese commercial treaty, most of them can no longer maintain their business. At the same time, the overseas Chinese who return to the country to invest in the area are also extorted by corrupt officials, making them unable to move forward or backward. They jointly suggested to the Central Government: 1. Please negotiate with the French authorities to conclude a new commercial treaty as soon as possible. 2. When overseas Chinese merchants return to the country to jointly run companies and purchase land, they are often reported as government property and occupied by powerful people and responsible officials. Please order them to be returned. 3. Any foreign commercial disputes cases that are submitted to the country for negotiation without the original case files from the responsible authorities shall not be accepted, so as to avoid confusion in jurisdiction. The Overseas Chinese Association has transferred the cases to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs according to their nature and submitted them to the Executive Yuan for approval. (Special dispatch, 25th)

National Economic Commission Plans to Hold a Plenary Session

(Nanjing) The National Economic Commission has not yet decided on the budget for the commission, and although the one-year work plan has been approved by the third standing committee meeting, it still needs to be decided by a plenary session. It is now planned to convene a plenary session to discuss progress. Standing Committee member Song Ziwen intends to enter Nanjing from Shanghai immediately. When the conference will be held will be decided after Song arrives in Nanjing. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Xi'an) Liu Jingshan, director of the Northwest Office of the National Economic Commission, telegraphed Shaanxi on the 24th, stating that he is scheduled to depart from Nanjing on the morning of the 25th and arrive in Shaanxi on the 27th. He will first establish an office and start with investigations. The authorities have sent a car to Tongguan to meet him. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

Siamese Overseas Chinese Urge the Government to Conclude a Commercial Treaty

(Nanjing) Siam has a population of 20 million, with 3 million overseas Chinese. The overseas Chinese have hundreds of schools in Siam, including 53 in Bangkok, such as the Chinese Middle School and the Overseas Chinese Middle School. Those who seek further education return to the country to enter Jinan University or Sun Yat-sen University Lingnan University. In recent years, the Siamese government intends to naturalize the Chinese into Siamese nationality. All schools are forced to learn Siamese, and when they reach a certain age, they must fulfill their military service obligations. Siam produces abundant rice, exporting tens of millions of piculs to various countries every year. Most of the rice mills in Siam were founded by the Chinese, and other businesses are also mostly run by the Chinese. As for Siamese people engaged in business, there are only a few in every hundred. However, China and Siam have no commercial treaty relationship, so the overseas Chinese in Siam are like nationals of countries with no treaty. Recently, tragic incidents have occurred, and the overseas Chinese feel more urgently the need to conclude a commercial treaty as soon as possible. They have repeatedly telegraphed and appealed in recent days. The government believes that the conclusion of a commercial treaty is a mutual agreement and cannot be established unilaterally, so the issue still requires considerable formalities. (Special dispatch, 25th)

Full Text of Constitution Preliminary Draft to Be Disclosed Soon

Soliciting National Criticism

(Nanjing) The formal draft of the constitution has been officially completed and is currently being organized. It will be completed soon. On March 1, the full text will be sent to various newspapers for disclosure to solicit national criticism. After one month, it will be submitted to the Yuan meeting for discussion. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Nanjing) The Constitutional Drafting Committee is organizing the clauses and is scheduled to publish them on March 1 to publicly solicit opinions for a period of one month. When the period expires, it will be collected, organized, and submitted to the General Assembly for discussion. The task of the Constitutional Drafting Committee has been completed, and it will be concluded within days. The staff will be reassigned separately. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

Now that the matter has been completed, he is returning to Nanjing from Xunyang on a China National Aviation Corporation plane. According to news from the ministry, Chen's trip to Jiangxi to see Chiang was to report on the naval situation and there were no other matters. (Special dispatch, 25th)

The Panchen Lama has agreed, but the time has not yet been determined. It is expected to be in early next month. Lin also intends to go there at that time. (Special dispatch, 25th)

The bureau will send personnel to depart within days to prepare with the finance departments of each province. (Special dispatch, 25th)

Yin Rugeng Goes to Gubeikou

Liu Youxun, Xu Shiying, and Others Accompanied Him

To Meet with Matsui to Discuss Transfer Procedures

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng went to Miyun with his entourage at 8 a.m. this morning. After lunch, he led Liu Youxun, Xu Shiying, and others to Gubeikou. On the 26th, he will meet with the Japanese representative Matsui to discuss the transfer procedures. It will be implemented on the 28th. Qiu Haoting, the magistrate of Miyun County, is scheduled to go to participate in the transfer ceremony on the 28th. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng and the head of the Japanese Chengde Special Service Agency, Nikaido, have agreed on a draft plan for the takeover of Gubeikou, consisting of five items, which have been passed by the provincial and municipal governments. The original text is scheduled to be officially announced by the Ji-Mi Commissioner's Office on the morning of the 26th. The main points of the content are to return the administrative part and police power of Gubeikou to China. The Japanese military agency stationed in Gubeikou will not withdraw temporarily because the houses outside the pass have not yet been completed. The office building of the Gubeikou Office has been negotiated with the Japanese side. The Guo family's house occupied by the Japanese regiment club in Hexi City will be vacated and used as a temporary office for the Office of the Director-General. (Special dispatch, 25th)

(Tianjin) On the 25th, Tao Shangming visited Shi Jinghuan, director of the Hebei Department of Industry, to discuss measures to prevent the Kai-Luan mine workers' unrest and the incitement of workers' strikes by a certain country. Tao is scheduled to go to Tangshan on the 26th and to Yuguan at the beginning of next month to negotiate the return of the Great Wall's large and small Sixteen Ridges and the withdrawal of Japanese-puppet agencies. (Special dispatch, 25th)

Liu Bandit Besieges Lushi County Town

Lingbao Turns From Danger to Safety, Luonan is Alarmed

Large Armies Gather in Tongguan and Shanzhou

Gao Guizi Goes to Lingbao to Command the Suppression

(Beiping) Liu Guitang's bandits, with about 5,000 men and women hostages, fled to Lushi on the evening of the 22nd and besieged the county town. Lingbao turned from danger to safety, and Luonan County in Shaanxi Province is in a state of emergency. Jiang Chuoou's armored car team chased to Lingbao, and Feng Qinzai's division is stationed along the Guandi Town area. Gao Guizi has gone to Lingbao to command the suppression of his six regiments. Large armies have gathered in Tongguan and Shanzhou. Defensive works have been built on the plateau outside the South Gate of Tongguan. It is reported that Liu's bandits are attempting to enter Sichuan and join the Reds. Their route seems to be one through Nanzheng and one through Laohekou. However, because there are many cavalry among the bandits and the mountain roads are difficult to travel, Shaanxi is deploying troops to intercept and attack. (Special dispatch, 25th)

Panchen Lama's Birthday Celebration Suspended

(Nanjing) Today is the Panchen Lama's 53rd birthday. Due to the national crisis, there should be no extravagance, so no celebration was held. The Panchen himself, starting at 8 a.m., led more than ten lamas in reciting longevity sutras in his residence. Dai Chuanxian also went to accompany the recitation. All central government agencies sent to congratulate and representatives were turned away. Only tea and refreshments were prepared by the temple to entertain them, with no other actions. Also, the Panchen is scheduled to continue reciting the Amitayus Sutra for one day on the 26th. (Special dispatch, 26th)

(Nanjing) The Panchen Lama's 53rd birthday on the 25th had its celebrations suspended. Guests who came to congratulate were still numerous and were served with tea and refreshments before departing. The Panchen spent the entire day on the 25th lecturing and praying with the lamas. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

Ministry of Industry Plans to Jointly Operate an Automobile Factory with Ford Company

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry plans to jointly operate an automobile factory with the American Ford Company in China. The capital is set at 4 million, with Ford responsible for 3 million and China responsible for 1 million. The automobiles produced will be purchased entirely by China. After three years, China will take over and operate it independently. Personnel have been sent to contact Ford's office in Shanghai, and a contract will be signed soon. (Special dispatch, 25th)

He Yingqin Goes Hunting at Longevity Hill

(Beiping) He Yingqin went to Longevity Hill with his entourage this morning to hunt and returned to the city in the afternoon. (Special dispatch, 25th)

Tianjin Da Zhong Bank Panic Subsides

(Tianjin) Da Zhong Bank continued to cash in notes today. By the evening, a total of 6,000 yuan had been cashed out. Together with yesterday, a total of more than 23,000 yuan had been cashed out. There was no longer a run on the bank this afternoon. The cause of the panic was that the old manager of the bank, Wang Yanqing, resigned, and Li Sihao succeeded him. The profiteers took the opportunity to spread rumors. (Special dispatch, 25th)

Both China and Eurasia Airlines Suffered Losses Last Year

(Nanjing) China National Aviation Corporation suffered losses of tens of thousands of yuan last year due to the small number of passengers and mail. Eurasia Aviation Corporation also suffered losses of tens of thousands of yuan due to the Xinjiang turmoil and the suspension of the Landi route for several months. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

Police Officer Academy Moved from Beiping to Nanjing

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Interior's Police Officer Academy has decided to move from Beiping to Nanjing, using the Soldiers' Bridge Cultural College as its school site. It will be transported south in two batches starting early next month. Faculty and students will be the first batch, and equipment and documents will be the second batch. The Ministry of Interior has requested the Ministry of Railways to provide free transportation. The Beiping campus will be handed over to the Real Estate Clearance Office for disposal. (Special dispatch, 25th)

Current Commentary

The Significance of Italy, Austria, and Hungary Joining Hands 恒

The Great War is over. Of those seeking Germany's resurgence, France is the most active. The harsh conditions imposed on Germany by the Entente were mostly at France's insistence. Austria's independence and the formation of the Little Entente also relied on France's efforts. Later, as time passed, Britain and Italy gradually developed goodwill towards Germany, often voicing support for it on the international stage. However, since the rise of Hitler in Germany, international perceptions have undergone another change. Those who previously sympathized with Germany have become increasingly suspicious. After Austria's sudden actions and the exposure of the National Socialist Party's plot to seize power, Italy, which is connected to Austria, felt particularly uneasy. Italy also initiated the proposal for Britain, France, and Italy to maintain Austria's independence. Now, Italy has further moved to join hands with Austria and Hungary, adding another formidable enemy to Germany besides its historic rival, France. This is truly a great misfortune for Germany's revival movement.

There are many reasons why Italy resolutely joined hands with Austria and Hungary, but the main reason was prompted by Germany's designs on Austria. During the Great War, Italy abandoned the Triple Alliance and joined the Entente, aiming to acquire all of Albania, southern Anatolia in Turkey, and expand its colonies in North Africa. However, after the war, it did not gain an inch of Turkish territory, nor did it possess Albania. Its previous confidence did not materialize. Nevertheless, its grand ambition to turn the Adriatic Sea into its own inland sea and its ambition to spy on the Balkan Peninsula have never been forgotten. Attempts to forcefully seize Fiume from Yugoslavia and manipulate Albania's politics are manifestations of this ambition. Its relentless desire for Yugoslavia is aggressive. Without the existence of the Little Entente, an Italian-Yugoslav war would have broken out long ago. Therefore, the Little Entente is a brilliant structure carefully constructed by French diplomacy, aimed not only at preventing the merger of Germany and Austria but also at obstructing the revival of the Austro-Hungarian Empire and suppressing Italy's development in the Balkans.

Therefore, for Italy, to seek future development, it must first start by breaking the Little Entente. To break the Little Entente's alliance, it must first connect with countries that share its interests. The country whose interests most closely align with Italy is Hungary today. After the collapse of the Austro-Hungarian Empire, much of its territory was incorporated into the Little Entente, and Hungary's borders were particularly severely cut. Railways, rivers, forests, and mineral resources that could be used for livelihood were mostly divided among the Little Entente, and as many as three million Hungarians were incorporated into other countries. The Adriatic coastline is occupied by Yugoslavia. The pre-war economic system was severely damaged. At the same time, the national borders were surrounded on three sides by the Little Entente, making it impossible to move. To alleviate its suffering, to avoid the oppression of the Little Entente, and to seek a way out, it is wise to unite with Italy. By doing so, it can not only resist the Little Entente politically but also rely on Italy's ports like Fiume for economic exchange. Next, Austria can ally with Italy. The benefits for Austria allying with Italy are the same as for Hungary. However, Austria has always considered merging with Germany to be advantageous, but its repeated attempts have failed, gradually leading to a change of heart. The recent failure of the Nazi Party's plot to seize power in Austria has further facilitated the rapprochement between Austria and Italy, leading to the current situation of Italy, Austria, and Hungary joining hands.

The possibility of cooperation between Italy, Austria, and Hungary exists, as mentioned above. However, without the Nazi Party's plot in Germany, their cooperation would not have been so rapid. The cooperation between Italy, Austria, and Hungary will inevitably threaten the Little Entente led by France and affect Franco-Italian relations. Therefore, Italy's desire to break the Little Entente has been long in the making, but its manifestation in reality is now for the first time. The reason for its previous hesitation was fear of criticism from France. Now, however, the German Nazi Party is bent on revenge, and France's security is constantly threatened. If the merger of Germany and Austria were to succeed, it would certainly be detrimental to France. Therefore, turning a blind eye to Italy's development in Central Europe is a last resort. Unless Germany slightly curbs its aggressive ambitions, France and Italy will not clash. Therefore, the current conflict between Germany and Austria is actually benefiting Italy, and Germany's revival will face even greater difficulties.

Conflicting Policies on Austria Deepen the Rift Between Italy and Germany

Military Group in the Danube Region

Major Source of Turmoil in Central Europe

Vienna Italy's Undersecretary of Foreign Affairs, Suvich, arrived here from the Hungarian capital at noon today. He hosted a banquet at the Italian Embassy for Prime Minister Dollfuss of Austria. After the banquet, they held talks to discuss the negotiations in Hungary and the recent events in Austria. Suvich left for his home country that evening. (Havas dispatch on the 24th)

(London) The differences between Italy and Germany regarding the Austrian issue have led to increasingly tense relations between the two countries, causing anxiety in European diplomatic circles. The main point of contention between the two countries is the independence of Austria. However, the issue of economic solutions in the Danube region has also deepened the rift between the two countries. Italy recently put forward suggestions on this matter, with the independence of Austria as an important condition, and opened a sea outlet for Austria and Hungary via Trieste or Fiume. The eyes of European leaders are now focused on Suvich, the Italian Undersecretary of Foreign Affairs. Suvich visited the capitals of Austria and Hungary a few days ago and then came to Vienna again today to have a long talk with Austrian Prime Minister Dr. Dollfuss at the Italian Embassy. The nature of the discussion has not been clearly stated, but according to unofficial sources, the possibility of forming an economic and military group among Austria, Hungary, and Italy was discussed. Suvich's return to Vienna was unexpected, causing anxiety in Berlin political circles. According to general opinion, the establishment of a new group in Central Europe and the Baltic Sea cannot contribute to the solution of the Austrian issue or promote European peace. It is also doubtful whether Dr. Dollfuss will gain the support of the Austrian people in the current negotiations. The restoration of Austria, in the eyes of the Germans, will become another major element of chaos in Central Europe. (Reuters dispatch on the 24th)

Rome Italian newspapers have unanimously defended Italy's policies toward Hungary and Austria, stating that Undersecretary of Foreign Affairs Suvich's visit to Hungary was decided long ago. The Little Entente countries should not be alarmed by this. Release of Russian Staff Opens Way for Softened Japanese Attitude Toward Russia

Hirota Takes Responsibility for Breaking the Deadlock

Efforts to Reopen Illegal Sale of the Railway Negotiations

(Moscow) A report from Boli says that six Russian staff of the Chinese Eastern Railway who were arrested last September have been released as a result of negotiations among representatives from the Soviet Union, Japan, and "Manchukuo" in Tokyo and Harbin. The Soviet side insisted that the release of the arrested personnel and the restoration of normal railway administration were prerequisites for reopening the negotiations on the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway. Therefore, the release of the six men means restoring the Chinese Eastern Railway to its rightful status as stipulated in the Beijing-Fengtian Agreement. The released personnel are free to return to their country, and their vacant positions will be filled by the Soviet side. As for the illegal agents appointed by the "Manchu" side during the conflict period, they will also return to their original posts. (TASS dispatch on the 24th)

(Tokyo) According to the Japanese Foreign Ministry, the illegal negotiations of the Chinese Eastern Railway by the Russian puppets have been completely suspended since last September when the puppet organization arrested Russian railway staff and demonstrated against Russia, and Russia revealed the Japanese puppet's plot to seize the railway, up to the present day. After Foreign Minister Hirota took office, he took on the responsibility of breaking the deadlock between Japan and Russia. As a result of several contacts with the Russian side, Hirota proposed the following compromise conditions:

(1) Regarding the six arrested Russian railway staff, the Russian side insisted on immediate release and reinstatement, while the puppet side insisted on appointing puppet staff to replace them. The stalemate could not be broken, so the Japanese side proposed a compromise: the puppet organization releases the arrested Russian staff, and Russia voluntarily recalls them to their country. Their successors will be Russian staff.

(2) The power to appoint and remove staff belongs to the board of directors, and the director of the management bureau cannot appoint or remove staff. This is to ease the claims of both sides.

The Russian side has accepted Japan's proposal, and the puppet country also released the Russian staff yesterday. After their successors take office, the conference can be reopened. Japan and the puppets hope to convene an illegal meeting on the 27th or 28th. (China United News dispatch on the 25th)

(Moscow) The release of six Russian staff of the Chinese Eastern Railway by the "Manchukuo" government has created a good impression in Moscow. People here believe that this is the starting point for the railway dispute between Russia and Manchuria to move from tension to relaxation, and the danger of conflict between Russia and Japan can also be reduced as a result. According to reports from Harbin, although the Russian staff have been released, they may be deported, and their duties will be handled by "Manchukuo" assistant staff until the railway board of directors appoints replacements. (Reuters dispatch on the 24th)

(Tokyo) When the Soviet Ambassador visited Foreign Minister Hirota on the 8th, he said that if "Manchukuo" released the Soviet staff of the Eastern Railway, the Soviet side would propose a new sale price to proceed with the Eastern Railway negotiations. Now that the Soviet staff in question have been released, negotiations on the Eastern Railway in Tokyo are bound to resume. Foreign Minister Hirota will convey this to the Russian Ambassador upon receiving formal notification from "Manchukuo." The Russian Ambassador will then report to his home government for instructions. After the resumption, the Russian Ambassador will propose a new price in Japanese currency. Therefore, the future negotiations will focus on how to bridge the gap between this new price and the price desired by "Manchukuo." (Electric Communication dispatch on the 25th)

(Harbin) The Soviet-Manchu border river navigation conference and the border survey committee were previously broken off due to the insincerity of the Soviet Union. The "Manchu" government was preparing to resolve it independently. However, yesterday, when diplomatic representative Shi Luben visited Russian Consul in Harbin, Slazitsky, to announce the release of the Soviet staff, the Russian Consul made an unofficial statement about these two conferences, expressing a willingness to convene them. The "Manchukuo" government, believing that the Soviet side has expressed sincerity and is preparing to convene the meetings, considers that this is enough to improve Soviet-Manchu relations and has decided to suspend independent action. Therefore, the above two meetings can be realized in the coming days.

(Electric Communication dispatch on the 25th)

Claims Expanding the Army is to Protect the Puppet State

(Tokyo) The Japanese government's latest transfer of military officers is the first since the appointment of Army Minister Hayashi. World Commerce Declines

League of Nations Publishes Statistical Report

(Geneva) The League of Nations Economic and Communications Section today released a report on the pessimism of the current state and future prospects of world commerce. After carefully examining last year's figures, while national trade has occasionally improved, international commerce has declined. The volume of goods exchanged between countries last year decreased by 30% compared to 1929, and its value decreased by half when calculated in currency. Gold countries mostly retained 35% of their 1929 trade value, while the United States retained only a quarter. Japanese experts estimate that Japanese trade decreased by about 12.5%, and Australia claims to have lost only 8%. (Reuters dispatch on the 24th)

Japanese Political Strife Rages On

Military and Financial Cliques Oppose Each Other

The Military Exposes the Sins of Financial Cliques and Political Parties on Disciplinary Grounds

Financial Cliques and Political Parties Attack the Military's Interference in Politics on Military Disciplinary Grounds

(Tokyo) The struggle between the Japanese military and financial cliques is intensifying in the 65th Diet. The financial cliques are pursuing the military with statements on military discipline issues and alienation between the military and the people. The military is exposing the irregularities of financial cliques and political parties on disciplinary grounds. The struggle between the two sides is at a standstill. In the early stages of the 65th Diet, Army Minister Araki resigned due to illness after being attacked by both financial cliques and internal factions. The financial cliques took the opportunity to pursue, seeming to have gained the upper hand. However, in early February, the military turned defense into offense and concentrated its efforts on attacking Commerce Minister Nakajima. It turned out that Nakajima, under the direction of the financial cliques, manipulated both the political and civilian parties to attack the military. The military hated this person very much and used the feudal forces of the Upper House to attack the irregularities of Commerce Minister Nakajima. Commerce Minister Nakajima could not withstand the pressure and resigned due to illness. The military took advantage of the victory to pursue further, again raising the corruption of Ministers Hatoyama and Mito. The purpose was to break the united military of the political parties, first split the Seiyukai, cause internal strife within the political parties, and then overthrow the cabinet in order to obtain the next government. The political parties have recently become aware of the conspiracy, and the Okamoto Inquiry Committee will also cancel its extreme policies to guard against the military's schemes and prevent the political parties from splitting themselves. However, the internal affairs of the Seiyukai are very complicated, making it difficult to guard against. It is difficult to predict who will win the struggle between the two sides at present. The internal situation is listed as follows:

President's Faction

The so-called President's Faction of the Seiyukai was formed during the era of President Tanaka. At that time, Suzuki wooed Hatoyama, Mori, Kuhara, Nakahashi, Yamamoto (Tei), Hata, Kawamura, Katsuta, Nakajima, Shimada, Matsuno, and Yamaguchi to oppose the Tokonami Faction. After Tanaka's death, Inukai was elected as President to prevent Tokonami from contending for the presidency. After Inukai's death in the May 15th Incident, Suzuki became President himself. At this time, the Kuhara Faction separated from the Suzuki Faction and established its own faction to compete with Suzuki. The important members of the current President's Faction are as follows: Hatoyama, Ando, ​​Ashida, Ono, Morita, Inuzaki, Ishizaka, Hoshijima, Kawamura, Shimada, Matsuno, Tanabe, Yamaguchi, Uehara, Shiga, Hirose, Tsuchikura, Okada, Murata, Kawakami, Kawashima, Wakamiya, Okada, Shimizu, Kumagai, Shibube, Miyakawa, Fujio, Mikami, Makino Kobayashi, Nakano, Ichinose, Wakamoto, etc., currently occupy the majority of the party's power.

Kuhara Faction

When General Tanaka served as President of the Seiyukai, half of its political funds were provided by Kuhara Fusanosuke, and half were paid out of the secret funds of the Army Ministry, which enabled it to maintain its power. Later, General Tanaka gradually lost his power after taking the blame for the Zhang Zuolin bombing incident. After General Tanaka's death, Kuhara approached the Suzuki Faction and opposed the Tokonami Faction. Its main figures are: Tsugumo, Nishikata, Fujii, Tako, Nishimura, Namba, Kuramoto, Tsusaki, and Iwasaki, etc. Its members are about 50 people. Kuhara himself is a second-rate military leader in Japan, with the Japan Industrial Company as its headquarters. Its financial strength is valued within the party.

Yamamoto Faction

The leader of the Yamamoto Faction is Yamamoto Teijiro. Yamamoto was previously the president of the Taiwan Sugar Company, exploiting the people of Taiwan to create his current position. He once served as Minister of Agriculture. After Tanaka's death, his assets were used up, and his power was not as good as before. The main figures under his faction are: Azuma, Sunada, Kono, Tatsukawa, and Takeda, only a dozen people. They often take a neutral attitude towards the Suzuki-Tokonami dispute.

Tokonami Faction

Since Tokonami left the Minseito and returned to the Seiyukai, he has formed his own faction within the party. Originally, Hatoyama, Kawamura, Mizuno, Katsuta, etc. were all members of the Tokonami Faction. Because Tokonami was fickle and unable to take on national affairs, they abandoned Tokonami and surrendered to the Suzuki Faction. Its main members are as follows: Kurazono, Higuchi, Kaneda, Haruna, Suzuki, Taki, Terada, Toyota, Togo, Nakamura, and Mori, etc. There are a total of 60 or 70 people in the same faction within the party, which is the largest force against Suzuki. Mochizuki, Okazaki, Mito, Hamada, Imai, Noda, and Yamamoto (Taro), who are known as the old Seiyukai faction, have recently gradually approached the Tokonami Faction.

Others, such as Maeda Yonezo, who claims to be neutral, is actually a member of the Suzuki Faction. Yamazaki, Kato, Kinoshita, and Azuma, although claiming to be neutral, are actually members of the Tokonami Faction. The truly neutral faction is Takahashi Korekiyo, Horikiri, and Oguchi, only a dozen people. (China United Press News)

(Tokyo) The Seiyukai's Great Union faction wants to use the power of united political parties to resist the military. Today's House and Outside Affairs General Meeting will formally recognize their actions. 14th Anniversary of the Founding of the National Socialist Party

Hitler's Speech Vigorously Denounces the Treaty of Versailles

National Fortune Can Only Be Recovered with Wartime Spirit

Looking Back to Encourage the Future

Supporting Peace No Less Than Others

Munich: Today, a meeting was held here to celebrate the 14th anniversary of the founding of the National Socialist Party. Premier Hitler attended the meeting and delivered a speech, stating that in 1920, the Chinese people first realized the harm of the Treaty of Versailles and knew that they were actually paying the price of peace with enslavement. Looking forward, they were filled with trepidation. From the beginning, we felt that this kind of fate could only be reversed with resolute resistance. However, the turning point in Germany's national fortune could never be achieved by those who plunged the country into suffering. The figures and parties of the past could not be the pillars of the country. New leaders were needed. These clean leaders came from the trenches, and could only come from there, because only those who had faithfully fulfilled their duties to the motherland for four and a half years could save the motherland. Only they could have the great power to organize the chaotic domestic affairs. Therefore, the German soldiers began to work, creating the National Socialist Party, and knowing that to seek a healthy future, they should not maintain parliamentary institutions, but should fight to the death against freedom and system. Therefore, apart from the Party, no other parties could be tolerated, and all unnecessary reconciliations were rejected in order to achieve the goal of all the people of the country being compatriots. But this could only be achieved by breaking down all previous barriers with the spirit of wartime, and only by combining nationalism and socialism could the strength of our people be drawn from the bottom of the abyss, and the most unified group in German history be created with sincerity. If backward celebrities are recruited, or there is no firm belief and fervent loyalty to the new movement, then victory will ultimately belong to us, because those who can only call on some leaders to support them will inevitably wander in the wilderness, and only those who can call on the people of the whole country to be their backing can obtain a new source of power. Therefore, obtaining the representatives of the new country and the future of Germany is the great work of our movement. Hitler then thanked 2,000 old comrades for their assistance, which led to today's success, but today is still the first stage of development, and the struggle after this cannot be slackened. In the end, he said that we will never allow the German people to waste their energy on civil war. Although we cannot have cannons, tanks, and airplanes today, there are still many peaceful undertakings to be done, because the whole country really wants to be our backing. Those who represent the whole country will not hesitate to take responsibility for war. Those who only get the support of a part of the people often try to consolidate their domestic position with foreign wars. We do not need foreign victories today to win the people's hearts, but only demand that this people be given the rights they deserve. We deeply feel the righteousness of this demand and dare to be proud of being fervent supporters of peace. (National Telegram, 24th)

(Berlin) German Premier Hitler issued a broadcast speech today to celebrate the 14th anniversary of the founding of the National Socialist Party. In the speech, he reiterated Germany's intention for peace, saying that politicians would not resort to national power until absolutely necessary. Hitler had a new request to the people, but did not indicate whether it was a plebiscite or another election. Celebrations will continue tomorrow. Hitler will speak in Munich and broadcast it to various places by radio. At that time, one million political leaders from various places who are tasked with spreading National Socialist ideology among the people will be guided by Hess in Munich by radio and swear an oath of loyalty to Hitler. (Reuters, 24th)

(Berlin) Fourteen years ago, Premier Hitler announced the 25 basic principles of the National Socialist Party in Munich. A commemoration was held today. In the evening, Propaganda Minister Goebbels gave a speech in front of 5,000 party members and party officials, saying that the martyrs of the National Socialist movement all possessed courage, and later party members should maintain it. He also said that the internal ranks of the National Socialist Party are clear and not confused at all. When applied to governing the country, it should also be like this. Goebbels then said, we should train party members to despise money. He also said, "The various parties belonging to the bourgeoisie have flexible goals, but the methods they use are very strict. The National Socialist Party reverses this approach, that is, the goals do not change, but the methods used can be flexible," and so on. (Havas, 24th)

Berlin State Opera Commemorates World War Dead Soldiers

President Attends with Cabinet Members

The Whole Country Flies Flags at Half-Mast

(Berlin) Today is the heroic memorial day for the two million German soldiers who died in the European War. Memorial ceremonies were held throughout the country, and public buildings everywhere flew flags at half-mast. Many private residences in Berlin hung national flags with black gauze outside their windows. A grand memorial ceremony was held at the Berlin State Opera. President Hindenburg wore his uniform, and most cabinet members and representatives of civil and military officials attended in person. The stage of the opera house was full of national flags and pine and cypress trees. At the opening, the German musician Beethoven's famous piece "Coriolanus" was played. Then, Defense Minister General von Blomberg gave a speech, praising the heroism of the German soldiers and Germany's peaceful aspirations. At the end of the ceremony, the famous musician Wagner's funeral music "Twilight of the Gods" was played, followed by the national anthem and the song of the National Socialist Party. President Hindenburg then inspected four companies of the National Defense Forces and 300 policemen under the "Unter den Linden," and finally laid a wreath at the memorial monument for the fallen soldiers. Large crowds gathered around the opera house and the Lustgarten. All the ceremonies in the opera house were transmitted outside the house by wireless loudspeakers. (Havas, 25th)

Development of German Trade Policy (German Dispatch)

How the various countries of the world have developed in trade policy during 1933 cannot be clearly understood without reviewing the events that have transpired in trade policy over the years. The World Economic Conference, or especially its failure, was indeed a major blow to the development of commercial relations. However, the reason for the incessant changes in the organization of the world economy has been around for quite some time.

The abandonment of the gold standard, which is of utmost importance to the world economy, the attempt at British economic solidarity, and the rise of Japan with its strong export industry, as well as the fact that all countries are seeking to avoid the accidental impact of other countries' development, all of these are major reasons why new methods must be devised to revive world commerce. In recent years, the protectionism continuously implemented by various countries will inevitably prompt each country to not cooperate with others in an emergency situation, making the unity of each national economy increasingly tight, and autarky will also expand day by day, eventually even returning to the primitive situation before ancient times. However, nations participating in world trade are unwilling to have this evolution, because although each country wants to make its national economy independent, they all understand that if the differences in climate and geography between regions and countries are to be eliminated, the industrial assistance of a new era in transportation and trade must be used to assist them. Even the spiritual success of other nations cannot be achieved without this. To create a situation in which international goods exchange can be enhanced under a strengthened national economy, experiments have been seen everywhere in recent years. However, as a result of all negotiations and meetings, countries have generally failed to anticipate the major changes that have occurred after the war. This is undeniable. On the other hand, economists in various countries still believe that the ideal solution is to restore a situation that is suitable for the conditions before the European war. However, one thing has been overlooked, that is, "all communication between nations must be suitable for their internal organization." For example, it is inconceivable for a nation with extreme economic freedom and no plans to have its national management relate to foreign trade. Conversely, it is also impossible for a national economy under economic planning to enter a free system in foreign trade without major setbacks. In essence, the major collapse of the world economy is ultimately a contradiction in economic organization and economic meaning. The economies of the 19th and 20th centuries all gradually developed through their own efforts to a state of equilibrium. Unfortunately, this economy was devastated by the previous great war. Subsequently, new production sites have emerged everywhere. However, their rise was neither under natural conditions nor without others competing, and even under national protection, or even under national coercion, they were able to achieve great success. The circumstances are as described above. However, it is obvious that no nation in the world is willing to have this newly created production subject to foreign competition, without resistance, and return to annihilation. In addition, the Treaty of Versailles, the special status of Soviet Russia, and the chaos in the Far East all hinder the restoration of the economic equilibrium to its previous state through its own efforts.

As the country occupying the widest ground in Europe vigorously implements state-run foreign trade, whether the above-mentioned equilibrium can be restored, and whether there is a possibility of restoration if only in Europe, economists with far-sighted plans will all question what has happened. The fact that Soviet Russia must have a special stance in its price calculation alone means that other countries have no ability to counteract it. Fortunately, thanks to the effective measures taken by the Soviet Russian commercial representative agencies, the world economy has not undergone fundamental changes solely due to the Soviet Russian problem. However, the changes in the Soviet Russian economy are only the most notable events in its evolution. In fact, there are other things that are also sufficient to promote the realization of the same destruction of economic equilibrium. For example, if a certain country has always imported huge amounts of food, it suddenly changes its course, increases its domestic food production, and makes its import demand only a fraction of its previous imports. Consider the results of Italy's food war, and you can infer others. Furthermore, if a supplier of goods to a certain country suddenly feels powerless and unable to accommodate a corresponding amount of exchange goods, all of these are sufficient to destroy the economic equilibrium, and are inevitable. To remedy this, for several years, loans have not been raised to make up for the negative numbers in commercial settlements. However, the supplier of goods repays the creditor, and the creditor uses it to pay for the goods supplied. In this way, the supplier of goods pays himself with his own funds. As a result, the countries involved suffer losses in their payment and commercial settlement, and the situation remains unchanged.

The 1933 Economic Conference attempted to eliminate this situation. However, for this purpose alone, the situation of each country pursuing its own interests and the lack of sincerity on all sides, and the common sacrifices for the nation, have been fully exposed. The experiment of devising a general compromise between the world and the international community has come to an end. The only result actually obtained by the World Economic Conference was not the elimination of obstacles, but only preliminary matters for world planned economy, such as the establishment of committees to discuss the production and distribution of wheat, sugar, wood, etc.

Shortly before the World Economic Conference, a tariff truce was established for a time. At that time, most countries participated. However, in the blink of an eye, several countries had already announced their withdrawal, so that the tariff truce was of little importance to trade policy. Because the World Economic Conference was fruitless, the stagnation in trade continued to develop, and the principled changes in trade policy followed. Although countries still formally maintain the principle of most-favored-nation treatment, some countries have changed their original intentions and implemented an import adjustment system (Kontigcntierung), thus reducing the effectiveness of the most-favored-nation treatment regulations.

Germany learned a lesson from the experience of the World Economic Conference, that is, it is difficult to find an international solution to the difficulties of various countries. Only through the healthy development of the national economy of each country can the crisis of the world economy be overcome. In view of this, Germany has devoted itself to the consolidation of its internal economy, and has made particular efforts to eliminate the huge unemployment problem and devise plans to revitalize the situation of farmers. The effects achieved have been very significant. For example, the number of unemployed has been reduced by 2.5 million. Market management and price management measures have further promoted German production to independence, no longer subject to the fluctuations of world market prices. The profitable German peasant economy has therefore also gained a foundation.

This approach has guided the production of industry towards improvement, and indirectly has benefited the development of German foreign trade. Although the index of German foreign trade once stopped falling in 1932, it continued to decline in 1933, and the decline was enormous, so that in 1933, Germany's exports were only half of the previous year's figure. The reason for this is that Germany has always refused to supply its currency standard to the experiment of trade policy. Important competing countries such as Britain, the United States, and Japan have all abandoned their gold standard and started a policy of devaluation dumping. At this time, Germany still maintains the gold standard of its currency. In this way, the export trade has been sharply reduced, and the foreign exchange deficit will inevitably rise with it. Germany was forced to implement foreign exchange controls, and in order to make foreign exchange easier to settle in terms of control, it had signed agreements with various countries on payment and settlement. Payment agreements can be divided into two types in form, namely, national agreements (that is, those signed between governments in the form of records) and bank agreements (that is, those agreed between the national bank and the banks of other countries issuing banknotes).

Seven Photographs of the Puppet Government Organized in Southern Xinjiang

This photograph shows the two puppet Tao-yins released by Tie Muer, the puppet leader during the rebellion, to Kashgar: (1) Su Jinshou (Hui Hui), (2) You Wenbin (Turban). Since Tie Muer's death, Su Jinshou has fled to Han City. Now the puppet Tao-yin of Kashgar is only You Wenbin. You's original name is You Luosi.

The purpose of the national agreement is to fundamentally abolish the foreign exchange restrictions on imports, and under this situation, to revitalize international goods communication. Importers use the funds to pay for the import of goods. If the maximum amount of foreign exchange exceeds the limit, an account can be opened at the bank issuing banknotes in that country, so that when continuing to import goods, it can be paid to the name of the account opened without restriction. The foreign bank issuing banknotes pays the creditors of foreign goods in the currency of that country, and uses the funds deposited in the name of the account to pay for German export goods. However, this agreement is only effective for countries that are not subject to foreign exchange pressure and have no compulsory economy. The intention of establishing a bank agreement is to make it easier for countries with weak foreign exchange to seek convenience in payment procedures with each other. The standard of payment of the signatory country is limited to the national currency of each country in the agreement. All import and export debts owed by both parties are settled by the bank. In this way, the numbers revealed in the monthly settlement can not only be offset against each other, but can also be completed. That is, the goods exported by that country to this country can also be paid for. For this reason, the trade communication between the two parties should be able to develop based on it.)

(National News Agency)

Chiang Kai-shek Rectifies the Administrative Commissioner System

Specifies Five Key Points for Handling Administration

Orders to the Provincial Governments of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi

Nanchang Dispatch: Chiang Kai-shek's headquarters believe that the provinces and regions of our country are vast, and there is a separation between the provinces and counties. It is difficult to take care of both the upper and lower levels. Therefore, the commissioner system was created. Since its implementation, the results have been gradually apparent. The system is still young, and old habits have not been eliminated. There are still inevitable Tao-yins who are regarded as unimportant in the past. Regarding the measures for suppressing bandits and local politics, and the reorganization of local finances, the provincial government and its subordinate offices and departments all directly issue orders to the counties, so that the commissioners are isolated and cannot fulfill their supervisory duties. Therefore, five key points for correction have been specified, and yesterday they were ordered to the provincial governments of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi to follow, in order to promote administrative efficiency. The original order reads, "The provinces and regions of our country are vast, and there is a separation between the provinces and counties. It is difficult to take care of both the upper and lower levels. Therefore, the commissioner system was created, in order to innovate and improve local politics. The regulations for the organization of the Supervisory Commissioner's Office were promulgated in the headquarters for suppressing bandits in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui. The significance of its creation was clearly indicated in the instructions and documents. Since its implementation, the results have been gradually apparent, which proves that the establishment of this commissioner is in line with the needs of the political environment. The system is still young, and old habits have not been eliminated. There are still inevitable Tao-yins who are regarded as unimportant in the past. Regarding the measures for suppressing bandits and local politics, and the reorganization of local finances, the provincial government and its subordinate offices and departments directly issue orders to the counties, so that the commissioners are isolated and cannot fulfill their supervisory duties. The original intention of establishing officials and creating systems has been lost. Corrections should be made urgently to promote administrative efficiency. The key points are listed as follows: (1) The provincial government or the competent offices and departments shall order all counties in the province to undertake important matters uniformly, and must supervise the districts separately and complete them within a time limit. The administrative supervisory commissioners shall be separately ordered and notified to order the counties under their jurisdiction, and shall be responsible for supervising the handling separately. (For example, organizing Baojia, promoting education, and other time-sensitive matters.) (2) When the provincial government or the competent offices and departments encounter special matters that must be handled by one county under the jurisdiction of a certain administrative region, the supervisory commissioners shall be separately ordered and notified to order the county to follow, and shall supervise the progress. (For example, suppressing bandits and clearing the countryside, completing warehousing, reforming malpractices, and other special matters.) (3) When the provincial government or the competent offices and departments encounter interconnected matters that must be handled jointly by the counties under the jurisdiction of Supervisory Commissioner A and Supervisory Commissioner B, the respective supervisory commissioners shall be separately ordered and notified to order the respective counties to follow, and shall jointly supervise the progress. (For example, blockading bandit areas, clearing the countryside and suppressing bandits together, repairing provincial roads, and other matters related to each other.) (4) In the case of the above three circumstances, the respective county governments shall submit the handling situation to the administrative supervisory commissioner in charge, and report it to the provincial government, and inform the respective competent offices and departments. (5) The actual situation of local fiscal revenue and expenditure in each county shall be reported to the administrative supervisory commissioner in charge on a monthly basis for verification. In addition to the separate orders, the above five points shall be ordered to the provincial government to follow, and shall be forwarded to the subordinates to follow. This order" (February 23)

Three Provincial River Associations Request Funds to Reorganize the Yellow River Embankment

Statistics Show a Need for More Than 12 Million Yuan

Jinan Dispatch: The three provinces of Hebei, Henan, and Shandong are located in the lower reaches of the Yellow River, especially Shandong Province, which has the longest section. It has been many years since the course was changed, and the siltation is getting higher and higher. Every time there is a flood. It was not until the year before last that the three provinces had the organization of the Yellow River River Affairs Federation to plan for unified flood control and repair. Last year, the river breached in southern Hebei, submerging western Shandong. The Stone Village mouth is still not blocked. Now that the ice flood has passed and the flood season is coming, how to reorganize the entire embankment and how to arrange the flood control project are all important. Last year, the third annual meeting of the Three Provincial River Affairs Conference was held in Jinan. It was resolved that the three provincial river affairs bureaus should separately estimate the work and prepare a plan. It was collected at the Shandong River Affairs Bureau in Jinan and compiled into a whole plan. It was presented to the five provincial governments of Hebei, Shandong, Henan, Jiangsu, and Anhui, and the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission, the Guidance Huai Committee, the Yangtze River Channel Engineering Committee, and the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee, a total of nine agencies. The current dangerous situation of the Yellow River was stated, and it was difficult to avoid accidents without a thorough reorganization. The south can submerge Jiangsu and Anhui, and the north can submerge Hebei and Shandong. The harm caused by the turbid current will be several times greater than the river breach in southern Hebei last year. Please present the case to the central government for approval and allocate funds for reorganization as soon as possible, etc. As of now, the three provinces of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan have completed the survey and estimation, and the engineering plans have been collected in Jinan. The post-disaster water control project of the Yellow River in Hebei Province is 1.89 million yuan. The post-disaster project of the Yellow and Qin Rivers in Henan Province is 4,633,040 yuan, 1 jiao, 7 fen, and 2 hao. The dam maintenance project in Shandong Province is 6.4 million yuan, totaling 12,923,040 yuan, 1 jiao, 7 fen, and 2 hao. All the presentations and consultations of the Three Provincial River Affairs Federation to the five provincial governments and the four water conservancy agencies have already been issued by the Henan River Affairs Bureau separately. The original text is as follows: "Case investigation of the third regular meeting, proposed by Chen Ruzhen, director of the Henan River Affairs Bureau, Sun Qingze, director of the Hebei Yellow River River Affairs Bureau, and Zhang Lianjia, director of the Shandong River Affairs Bureau, that the association should submit to the five provincial governments of Jiangsu, Anhui, Henan, Hebei, and Shandong to request the central government to approve a huge amount of money to repair the embankments of the three provinces. The details are as follows: In the proposal, the embankments of the three provinces of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan are the screens of North China and the guarantee of the southeast, and are of great importance. However, they have been in disrepair for many years, the riverbed is getting higher and higher, and the embankment is getting lower and thinner. The dangerous situation is already precarious. After the autumn flood this year, the water was washed away, and the low places are even more so, resulting in many breaches, which is a warning in fact. If we do not seek remedy and reorganize properly, the disaster will be unimaginable in the future. It is better to prepare for the rain and repair in advance for safety, rather than breach the embankment and let the lives and property of hundreds of millions of people sink to the bottom, and then spend a lot of money to plan for blocking. The advantages and disadvantages are obvious. Ruzhen and others are responsible for keeping silent and feel uneasy. It is proposed that the association submit to the five provincial governments of Jiangsu, Anhui, Henan, Hebei, and Shandong to request the central government to approve a huge amount of money to actively repair and maintain the river defense and protect the people's livelihood. Is it appropriate? Please make a public decision, etc. The conference decided that the river affairs bureaus of each province should prepare plans and charts and send them to the association for compilation and presentation to the provincial governments and the competent authorities of the river affairs bureaus, and forward them to the central government for rapid handling, in order to facilitate river defense and protect the lives of the people, etc. The records were passed. The association has reviewed this case, and now the embankments of the three provinces of Henan, Hebei, and Shandong are indeed getting lower and thinner. If we do not actively repair and maintain them, and there is any neglect, the south breach will inevitably take the Huai River into the Yangtze River. Not only the diversion and diversion plan, and the Yangtze River project, will be completely abandoned, but also the people of the three provinces of Henan, Anhui, and Jiangsu will suffer. The north breach will inevitably cut off the Pinghan Jinpu, cross the Wei River, and enter the sea through the canal. Not only the Haihe project for many years will be destroyed, but also the people of the three provinces of Henan, Hebei, and Shandong will be harmed endlessly. It is now approved that the river affairs bureaus of the three provinces have prepared plans and charts, and have sent them to the agency one after another. The original plans and charts should be checked and presented to your government for approval and forwarding to the National Government and the Executive Yuan, and a huge amount of money should be allocated as soon as possible, so that they can be actively repaired and maintained as soon as possible, in order to maintain river affairs and protect the lives of the people. It is a public convenience. Sincerely presented to Han, chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, Yu, chairman of the Hebei Provincial Government, Liu, chairman of the Henan Provincial Government, Chen, chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, Liu, chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, and Li, chairman of the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission."
