Aftermath of a Honey Trap

Chen Fuliang Originally Sentenced to Two Months in Prison

Sentence Increased to One Year Imprisonment After Appeal

Previously, Lin Yaoxuan, a Sichuan native, residing in room 37 of Yiji Sichuan Warehouse, No. 1 Huicheng Lane, Madian Road, French Concession, 28 years old, frequently traveled between Sichuan and Shanghai, dealing in white fungus, pickles, and foreign goods. He was quite wealthy. He lived in Shanghai for many days and often felt lonely. He occasionally visited prostitutes. Hu Ruiting, a foreign goods broker from Zhenjiang who knew him, introduced Ms. Wu, the wife of Shen Shoukang, the owner of the Jiankang Hospital at No. 25 Avenue Joffre, French Concession, to Lin as a mistress. They often used hotels as a place for secret trysts. At about 2:00 p.m. on September 29 of last year, Hu ordered Ms. Wu to go to room 532 of the Central Hotel in the Public Concession first, and invited Lin to continue their rendezvous. Shen Shoukang, Ms. Wu's husband, found out about it and discussed it with his friend Chen Fuliang. Chen then led Shen and his companion Li Hong to the Central Hotel, broke into the room, and accused Lin of adultery in order to extort money (commonly known as a "honey trap"). First, they slapped and beat Lin, and then Chen and others took Lin to the law office of Zhang Wei at No. 105 Xuehuali Road, French Concession, and confined him. They threatened him in every way, forcing him to issue two promissory notes for 500 yuan each, totaling 1,000 yuan, with a deadline of October 1 for payment to settle the matter. They also took away 15 yuan in cash and a watch from Lin's person before releasing Lin and restoring his freedom.

Later, Lin was unwilling to accept this and reported to the French police station, accusing Chen and others of kidnapping and extortion and requesting prosecution. The police chief approved the report and sent detectives to arrest Chen, Shen, Li, Hu, and Ms. Wu and to search Chen's house and retrieve the promissory notes, cash, and watch. They were sent to the Second Special District Local Court for prosecution. After trial, Shen Shoukang and Chen Fuliang were each sentenced to two months in prison and fined 200 yuan each. Li Hong was sentenced to two months in prison, and Hu Ruiting was fined 300 yuan. Shen Wu was acquitted. Shen Shoukang was granted a two-year suspended sentence. During the appeal period, they were all allowed bail. Later, Li and Hu expressed their willingness to accept the sentence, and the sentence has already been executed after being confirmed. However, Chen Fuliang alone expressed his disagreement with the original sentence and hired a lawyer to appeal to the Jiangsu Higher Third Branch Court.

The above-mentioned situation has been reported in the previous newspaper. After repeated hearings by the High Court, the final verdict was announced in the Third Criminal Court by Judge Guo, accompanied by Assessors Fan and Sun, and Chief Prosecutor Zhao, the day before yesterday afternoon. Chen was summoned to court. The judge read out the main text of the judgment, the original judgment was revoked, and Chen Fuliang was sentenced to one year in prison for joint intimidation and extortion. The number of days of detention before the judgment was determined will be offset at two days per one day of imprisonment. After the judgment, the judge explained the meaning of the judgment to Chen, saying that the court's trial result showed that your criminal acts were organized and planned, and the original trial's sentencing was inappropriate, so the sentence was changed to one year in prison. If you disagree, you can appeal to the Supreme Court within ten days of receiving the judgment. You failed to appear the last two times you were summoned, and the bailor also failed to appear in court. This court believes that you have a risk of escape and must be taken into custody today. When Chen heard the order to be taken into custody, his face changed and he asked to remain on the original bail or to find another suitable bailor. The court did not allow it, and the police took him to the detention center for custody.

Prostitute Sues Zhang Zhiliang for Abandonment After Love Affair

Zhang Denies Cohabitation

Verdict Scheduled for March 1

Han Xiaomao, a Suzhou native and prostitute from Changsan Brothel [high-class brothel], also known as Yan'e Lao Ba, 22 years old, is currently at Qunyufang, and seeks cases under the name "Li Qing". Through her lawyer, Han lodged a complaint in the criminal court of the Second Special District Local Court accusing Zhang Zhiliang, a native of Chuansha, 31 years old, who resides at No. 1 Xingshun North Lane, Remi Road, French Concession, and runs a construction factory (the factory's name is unknown), of seducing and abandoning her, a violation of Article 310 of the criminal law.

The complaint stated that in the spring of 1913, when she was 18 years old, she met Zhang Zhiliang. Because she was young and inexperienced and her will was weak, she was seduced by Zhang into committing adultery. Because she was six months pregnant, she married Zhang as a concubine. She lived with Zhang in his house in Chuansha, Pudong. After three months, she gave birth to a daughter. At first, they were on good terms, but unexpectedly, over time, Zhang became tired of her and treated her with violence. The following year, when she returned to Ningbo to visit relatives, Zhang refused to cohabitate with her. She had no choice but to return to Shanghai and live with her mother. Since then, Zhang has not provided any living expenses. The defendant has abandoned her, violating the criminal law, and should be investigated. In addition, she filed a civil suit to recover the debts incurred by the plaintiff and her daughter for living expenses during the period of abandonment, as well as the living expenses for the next 39 years of the plaintiff's life until the age of 60 and the daughter's education expenses, totaling 87,860 yuan.

According to the complaint, the court summoned the plaintiff, Han Xiaomao, and her lawyer to the Second Criminal Court the day before yesterday by Presiding Judge Wu Fanglian. Han Xiaomao testified that she was seduced by Zhang in the first month of her eighteenth year. In August of that year, she married Zhang as a concubine and lived with him in Yile Lane, Danshui Road. In November, she gave birth to a daughter. In February of the following year, Zhang and his second concubine took her to Zhang's house in the countryside, where they lived for two months. After returning to Shanghai, she was abandoned and ignored.

The defendant, Zhang Zhiliang, and his defense lawyers, Wang Shizong and Zhu Taiqing, arrived in court. Zhang stated in his defence that the plaintiff was known as Yan'e Lao Ba in the brothel in the winter of 1912, and he and his friends met her during a call. In the spring of 1913, the plaintiff opened her own brothel, renamed herself Zhuo Wenjun, and due to pregnancy at Mid-Autumn Festival she stopped her visits, and lived in Yile Lane. He often went to her home to see her. After she gave birth, in the spring of 1914, she worked as a prostitute in Sanyuanfang, renamed herself Wen Di, and then sought cases at Fuxiang Lane, changing her name to Hua Bifang. Recently she was known under the name Li Qing in Qunyufang. He never married her as a concubine, nor did they cohabitate. Her daughter was not his. Completely false accusation and requested to be acquitted, and requested permission to countersue the plaintiff for slander. He named his friends Zhu Xiaofeng (manager of the real estate department of Wuhe Foreign Company) and Zhu's concubine Cui Meimei, as well as his own second concubine Yao Jinying, as witnesses.

The three witnesses gave their statements, Zhu said that he had gone to the plaintiff's place with Zhang Zhiliang for social entertainment, but did not know that Zhang had married the plaintiff as a concubine. Cui's testimony was the same as her husband's. Yao Jinying stated that Zhang Zhiliang was her husband, and she lived at No. 1, Lane 107, Songshan Road. She did not know the plaintiff and had seen her once. According to her husband, she was the wife of a friend. After the lawyers on both sides debated, the court adjourned the debate and scheduled the verdict for 9:00 a.m. on March 1.

Intense Courtroom Debate Over the Auction of Huang Chu-jiu's Real Estate

Judge Cao Advocated Transferring the Property to Mortgagees at an Assessed Price

Attorney Yan Firmly Opposed, Requesting Auction by an Auction House

丨The Debate Remained Inconclusive, Rescheduled for Further Hearing丨

Following the death of Huang Chu-jiu and the subsequent collapse of Gongfa Company, Daye Bank, and the Great World Entertainment Deposit Department, the litigation over his debts and estate has not been fully resolved. The Second Special District Court held another execution hearing the other day regarding the auction of Huang's real estate, summoning both creditors and debtors to express their opinions. The courtroom proceedings are recorded as follows: After the court was called to order, the attorneys representing both the creditors and debtors were summoned to the court. Judge Cao Jun announced that the court had repeatedly auctioned Huang Chu-jiu's real estate at reduced prices. Only one property in Rongqing Lane and one leased land on Avenue Foch had been purchased. The rest remained unsold. The court now intends to transfer the real estate to the mortgagees at an assessed price. Attorney Yan Luqing, representing the creditors, immediately stood up to object, stating that his clients had submitted a petition to the court, and he was unsure if it had been received. He then read the entire draft of the petition verbatim. The petition stated:

(The petition reports unfounded rumors. The petitioners are impoverished and helpless creditors of Daye Bank. Since the death of Huang Chu-jiu and the subsequent collapse of Daye Bank, three years have passed. Only 20% of the debt has been repaid by the former French Concession court. Since the case was taken over by this court, two years have passed, and not a single penny has been repaid. With regard to the sale of Huang Chu-jiu's real estate, the petitioners have submitted dozens of requests to designate an auction house for the auction. However, this court has disregarded the petitioners' wishes and conducted the auction itself. The result is exactly what the petitioners predicted: a waste of time and advertising expenses. Moreover, the delay has led to rent reduction issues, greatly diminishing the value of the real estate. Recently, we have heard the following unfounded rumors, which have left the petitioners distraught: "Regarding the Huang Chu-jiu case, the judge of the execution court of the Second Special District Court is a living Bodhisattva, no different from a puppet. It is said that Wanchun Banking Group (whose mortgage contract, though bearing the names of prominent figures in Shanghai, is suspected of being forged and is well-known to the court) and the China Industrial Bank (whose mortgage contract for banknotes has long expired) have reached an agreement with the president of the court to utilize the regulation that appeals do not suspend execution of the case, allowing them to receive the existing funds in the court." Upon hearing this, the petitioners were dubious and rushed to their attorney, Yan Luqing, inquiring whether the rumors were reliable and requesting the court to conduct a thorough investigation. Attorney Yan stated, "These rumors are unreliable and damage the reputation of the court. It is regrettable that the creditors did not send the rumor-mongers to the Public Security Bureau for strict punishment according to law. As for Wanchun Banking Group and China Industrial Bank wanting to receive funds, the execution court will definitely not allow it. Please rest assured. Although Wanchun Banking Group and China Industrial Bank have requested payment, since the creditors have expressed their opposition, the court will order Wanchun Banking Group and China Industrial Bank to file a lawsuit for confirmation and will not rashly approve their payment. This is the legal point of view. In fact, the president of the court is as intelligent and wise as this attorney. If I were in his position, I would not allow the payment either. If the Wanchun Banking Group and China Industrial Bank are recklessly allowed to receive the money and leave, it will not benefit the court and will impose a significant responsibility. Who would be willing to do this? Even a madman would not be willing to do it. Would a president of the court who is intelligent and upright be willing to do this? It is self-evident. Moreover, even if all of Huang Chu-jiu's real estate is sold, the proceeds would not be sufficient to satisfy the claims of Wanchun Banking Group and China Industrial Bank. The ordinary creditors of Daye Bank would not receive a single penny. Therefore, the court will definitely not recklessly approve the payment. As for the creditors' request for the court to thoroughly investigate this rumor, it is meaningless. Wanchun Banking Group and China Industrial Bank have not contacted the president of the court to receive payment. Furthermore, the court will definitely not allow Wanchun Banking Group and China Industrial Bank to receive payment. Therefore, these unfounded rumors will disappear without investigation." Upon hearing this, the petitioners thanked him and retreated. We now submit this petition, earnestly requesting the execution court of this court to reject the payment requests of Wanchun Banking Group and China Industrial Bank. The petitioners would rather lose in the civil court. This is for the public good. Respectfully submitted to the execution court of the Second Special District Court of Shanghai.)

After Attorney Yan finished reading the petition, the entire courtroom was silent. Judge Cao took the petition to read it and then stated that the petition mainly contained two points. The first point was the request for auction by an auction house, and the second point was the opposition to the mortgage claims of China Industrial Bank and Wanchun Banking Group. Regarding the auction issue, it could be discussed. Attorney Shan Yuhua, representing the mortgagee China Industrial Bank, stated that the China Industrial Bank was willing to receive the real estate at an assessed price, as instructed by the court. Attorney Peng Qi, representing the mortgagee Wanchun Banking Group, stated that Wanchun Banking Group was unwilling to receive it. Attorney Yan stated that China Industrial Bank and Wanchun Banking Group were not qualified to express their opinions before their claims were confirmed. Attorney Shan then debated with Attorney Yan. Attorney Yan reiterated that the court had previously conducted the auction of Huang Chu-jiu's real estate itself, but no one had purchased it, as the creditors had predicted. This was due to two reasons: First, the auction procedures of the judicial authorities were cumbersome. Second, it was due to the prevailing superstition in our country that purchasing property from the judicial authorities was unlucky. To ensure the early sale of Huang Chu-jiu's real estate and obtain a higher price, it was necessary to designate an auction house for the auction. Moreover, the method of designating an auction house for the auction had been requested by the majority of creditors. Previously, the court had granted the request of a minority of creditors and conducted the auction itself, resulting in a waste of time and advertising expenses. Therefore, today, the court should grant the request of the majority of creditors and designate an auction house for the auction. Furthermore, this case was a special case in Shanghai and should be handled specially. Attorney Zhu Shuzhen then stated that Attorney Yan's proposal to have the auction house conduct the auction was not unreasonable. Previously, Huang Chu-jiu's movable property had also been auctioned by an auction house designated by the court. Therefore, it would not be inappropriate for the court to hand over the real estate to the auction house for auction and see how it goes. Attorney Shan stated that the case had already been auctioned at a reduced price, and it was inconvenient for the court to come forward for the auction again. The liquidators Wu Zheng, Pan Zhaobang, and the accountant could join Attorney Tan Yigong to publish an auction advertisement. Attorney Tan stated that Attorney Shan was unaware of the complexity of the case, and it was inconvenient for him to come forward. Accountant Pan stated that the case had already been auctioned at a reduced price, and no one had purchased it. It would be better to transfer the property to the mortgagees at an assessed price, as instructed by the court. Attorney Yan stood up angrily and loudly requested the clerk to record that anyone requesting to transfer the property to the mortgagees at an assessed price should be recorded in the minutes. If the property was transferred to the mortgagees at an assessed price, the ordinary creditors would not receive a single penny. Therefore, the creditors would have to settle accounts with those requesting to transfer the property to the mortgagees at an assessed price. Attorney Yu Zhongluo stood up and stated that Attorney Yan's angry and aggressive presentation was inappropriate. Attorney Yan stood up and stated that he was fighting vigorously with anger because he saw that his clients' rights were in danger. Even if it violated etiquette, he did not care. Accountant Pan then declared to the court that he was withdrawing the above proposal and requested the clerk to record the withdrawal request in the minutes. At this point, Judge Cao adjourned the court and announced that a further hearing would be scheduled. The intense debate was finally calmed.

The Shanghai Chinese Public Bus Company Believes the Time is Premature to Extend Bus Service to Wusong

The Company Replied to the Public Utilities Bureau by Letter

Since the Shanghai Chinese Public Bus Company received orders to extend the Shanghai-Wusong line, it has now learned that the company has submitted a report. The original text is as follows: Regarding the matter of submitting a reply, the instruction No. 2605 issued by your bureau on February 12th stated that the Seventh District Party Headquarters requested to instruct the company to extend Route 4 to Wusong, etc. Upon receiving this, we were about to reply when we received instruction No. 2608 from your bureau on February 15th, stating that according to the instruction of the Municipal Government and the approval of the Municipal Executive Committee, the matter of extending the public bus service to Wusong should be reported together for review. Upon receiving this, the company complied with the order and sent personnel to conduct a route survey and investigate the residents along the way to facilitate implementation. It was found that the length of the line from the New Municipal Government to the Aquatic School at Paotaiwan was 18 kilometers, and the road surface was all cinder, which was still rugged and uneven. In Yinhang Town, there were approximately 5,000 residents, and most of them were farmers engaged in agriculture. Furthermore, according to a certain gentleman from the Municipal Affairs Branch Committee of the town, there was already a taxi service station in the town, with two vehicles capable of accommodating a dozen people. However, there were very few passengers traveling from the city center to Shanghai. In Wusong Town, Paotaiwan, Zhanghuabang, and other places, more passengers took the small train than the municipal ferry. The municipal ferry departs once every hour, while the small train departs 19 times a day, and each train uses double engines. However, passengers tend to prefer the small train, and the number of passengers still seems uneconomical. The company sent personnel to investigate twice, and the reports were all consistent. Furthermore, the transportation from Wusong Town to the city center can be done by taking the small train to Jiangwan or Tiantong'an Station, and then transferring to the company's public bus, costing only 35 cents, which can be reached in less than an hour. The time and fares are both economical. It is also reported that the Beijing-Shanghai Railway is preparing to increase the number of trains in March, and at the same time, cancel seat classes and reduce fares. The municipal government has also approved the Ministry of Railways to extend the Shanghai-Wusong line to Sanmin Road, which has been reported in the newspapers and has already been implemented. The company repeatedly considered that if Route 4 were to be extended to Paotaiwan, it would inevitably require adding more vehicles to operate, which would be convenient. In addition, the road surface is uneven, and the machinery is prone to damage, which would further create competition between the company and the railway. If there are not enough passengers, both sides will suffer losses. Moreover, the railway is state-owned and has unlimited financial resources. The company is afraid that it will not be able to afford the sacrifice. The company believes that the time for extending public bus service to Shanghai-Wusong Town is still too early. We now submit this report with the actual situation, and we respectfully request your review and reporting for your convenience. Respectfully submitted to Xu, Director of the Public Utilities Bureau.

Dispute Over Restrictions on Rickshaw Licenses by the French Authorities

Since the French Concession Municipal Council implemented restrictions on rickshaw licenses in 1934, some rickshaw dealers did not receive the news in advance, resulting in all the licenses being pre-emptively obtained by major rickshaw dealers in the Nantao area. Some small rickshaw dealers who had only one or two rickshaws were unable to obtain licenses. There were more than 300 rickshaws affected. Since this incident occurred, more than three months have passed. Representatives of the rickshaw dealers have repeatedly been running around appealing and asking the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the French Concession to intercede with the French authorities on their behalf. The French Municipal Council replied that the original number of licenses was 17,000, and there were still 36 licenses remaining. The reason for the restriction was that the Board of Directors had approved the implementation and followed the example of the Public Concession in order to maintain traffic. The rickshaw dealers learned that 36 licenses were not enough to be distributed, so they unanimously refused to accept them. On the one hand, members of various rickshaw guilds conducted investigations and found that the association's report for January included 813 new members. However, the guild did not maintain the livelihood of old members and gave priority to new members in obtaining licenses, which was disregarding the suffering of fellow members. Therefore, hundreds of rickshaw pullers who have been unemployed for days have gathered in the guild in Sanminfang, Nantao, demanding that the guild find ways to provide relief. Upon learning of this, the committee members, fearing something unfavorable would happen, all avoided attending meetings and handling affairs, allowing the unemployed people to argue with each other. However, in order to seek relief for themselves, the rickshaw dealers convened a meeting yesterday to discuss countermeasures and elected Li Bingyi, Liu Qikuan, and Lu Xiushan as general representatives to handle all negotiation procedures. It was decided to question the guild for its poor handling of affairs with ten reasons, demanding a response within 48 hours; otherwise, a petition would be submitted to a higher authority. Regarding the method of requesting the French authorities to issue licenses, it was decided to: (1) Request the French authorities to re-register all rickshaws in order to identify those who obtained licenses by false pretenses. (2) Investigate and verify those who obtained licenses by false pretenses and file lawsuits against rickshaw dealers for compensation for losses incurred over the past three months according to law. (3) If the French authorities cannot relax the restrictions on rickshaw licenses, please extract one license out of every twenty licenses from major rickshaw dealers, based on a value of five percent. (4) Periodically go to the French Municipal Council and the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the French Concession to continue petitioning for relief for the livelihood of small rickshaw dealers and the poor. (5) Issue a declaration requesting assistance from all sectors of society. (6) Hire Attorney Wu Kaisheng as the representative of the unemployed rickshaw pullers to legally protect their rights. (7) Demand that all members of the guild provide mutual assistance to unemployed fellow members; otherwise, payments should be suspended, as the guild employs staff with huge salaries but does not handle affairs for members. (8) Before the dispute over rickshaw licenses is resolved, all rickshaw dealers should suspend the acceptance of March rickshaw licenses and wait for a fair decision from the French authorities. All the above measures were unanimously approved and adopted, and it was decided to gather at the guild hall in Sanminfang at 3 PM every day to discuss all the implementation measures. Therefore, the rickshaw license dispute may not be resolved for a while.

Reading Q&A

Can't Understand International Economic News (2)

The questions asked in the letter are answered in detail below:

(1) The purpose of the "Reading Guidance" founded by the circulating library of this newspaper is not only to serve the readers of this library but also to help all those who have dropped out of school and are eager to read to solve their reading problems. We believe that if we want the public to truly benefit from the library, it is not enough to simply provide many books. Given the current low level of culture among the general public, we have the task of helping readers select reading materials and solve reading problems. Therefore, we dare to take the risk of creating this kind of undertaking. Of course, this is a very difficult task. There is no precedent to follow and there is a lack of available reference materials. All of our work is in the trial stage. Therefore, we dare not make the scale very large at the beginning. We need to try it for a period of time to see how the results are before we dare to talk about development and popularity. We stipulate that participants are temporarily limited to the readers of this library, which is a helpless difficulty. However, we still hope to help those who cannot participate in the research of this department. Therefore, the "Reading Q&A" published in this newspaper is not limited to those who participate in the research of this department. All letters with stamps affixed to this column and whose questions are reading problems will be answered by this department, and those that are generally relevant will be published in the newspaper. Mr. Chen and readers who want to know more can refer to the "Reading Q&A Regulations" of this newspaper on January 4th of this year (published after the local news) and the "Origin of Reading Guidance" in the compilation of the library's book catalog.

(2) Regarding the inability to understand terms and new nouns encountered in reading newspapers, we feel that there are indeed many people who feel this kind of pain. To solve this difficulty, we feel that we can only diligently look up dictionaries (see "The Use of Dictionaries" in this column on February 9th and 10th). However, judging from the questions asked by Mr. Chen, relying solely on looking up dictionaries is still not enough, because the difficulty lies in the lack of basic knowledge and the lack of browsing of newspapers and magazines. For example, in the several nouns cited by Mr. Chen, in addition to "Gold Embargo Lifted" and "Gold Export," the literal meaning of "The United States Buys Gold" and "Devaluation of the US Dollar" can also be understood. The reason why Mr. Chen does not understand is the questions "Why does the United States want to buy gold?" and "Why is the US dollar devalued?" Therefore, in order for Mr. Chen to solve these problems, he still needs to first read one or two books on the principles of the subject and read more newspapers and magazines. Social science can be roughly divided into two aspects: one is to describe social phenomena; the other is to explain or analyze social phenomena. The former is a narrative of facts; the latter is an analysis and explanation of the content or nature of facts. For example, "The United States Buys Gold" is a fact, while "Why does the United States want to buy gold" is an explanation of the content of the fact or the nature of the problem. We see people "performing magic tricks" and find it very mysterious, but if someone explains to us the techniques of "performing tricks," it is not surprising at all. Therefore, to study social phenomena, we must pay attention to observation, that is, know more about the actual situation, because it is very dangerous to understand theory without empirical evidence. However, if you don't understand the theory and only observe the facts, it is like watching "magic tricks." You only know that it is very "mysterious" but you don't understand it. This is the first point that Mr. Chen and those who feel the same way should pay attention to.

Society is constantly changing. It is definitely not stagnant. Therefore, new events are constantly occurring in society, especially in this era of great social change. As a result, "new nouns" or "modern language" are increasing day by day. For example, "Currency Agreement," "Gold Embargo Lifted," and "Gold Policy" are all facts that have occurred in modern times and now. To understand the meaning of these nouns, the first is to look up a dictionary, and the second is to read articles in current affairs magazines related to these kinds of nouns (because the words in the dictionary are added one by one, and the facts that happened at that time are rarely added to the dictionary immediately. And the news in the newspaper only explains the outline of the facts, so to know the elucidation of the content of the facts, you must read magazines.) This is the second point that should be paid attention to.

Now let me introduce a few more books:

(A) General Theory. When studying economic phenomena, you should first read an overview book. Chen Baoyin's translation of the "Outline of Economics" (Lequn Edition) is a relatively complete reading material and is worth reading. However, this book is more in-depth. You should first read Chen Baoyin's "System of Economic Phenomena" (Lehua Edition). After that, if you like to study currency, you can read Hilferding's "Finance Capital" (Shenzhou Guoguang Society has a translated version, titled "Financial Capital"). As for the books you mentioned, they can only be used for reference later and should not be read when starting. In addition, you should also understand the current economic situation. After reading the above books, you will have a foundation in principles, but you still don't know the recent economic situation. Therefore, you should also read some books that explain the economic situation in recent years. Volga has a book "World Economy and Economic Policy" every year. Volga is a famous economist of the present era. His analysis can be said to be relatively accurate. So you should read it. Chinese translations of this book from 1929 and 1932 have already been published. (The former is the Shuimo Edition and the latter is the Shenzhou Edition).

(B) For dictionaries, you can refer to the books listed in the article "The Use of Dictionaries" on February 21st. I won't repeat them here. There are many domestic magazines about general current affairs. If you want to read them all, it will not only cost countless time and money, but it is also unnecessary. Therefore, you usually only need to read one or two kinds of magazines, such as the "Shen Bao Monthly" and the "Current Affairs Compilation." For other magazines, you can look for them at any time based on the topics you need to study. It is best to buy a "Periodical Index" (published by the Zhongshan Cultural Education Center) because this publication can tell you: which magazines have the topics you want to read.

Regarding the approach to studying "economics" and which books to read, this department has now commissioned experts to write "Economics Research Methods" to provide a systematic and correct indication for readers' reference. You can purchase it after it is published. However, according to your situation, you can read the books introduced earlier when you start.

Spring and Autumn

Science

— Yongzi

Science was originally a tool for solving all the mysteries of the natural world, but unfortunately, in this day and age, science itself has become a mysterious riddle. Look, with two wings and a motor, you can cross the Atlantic. Put up an antenna, turn on the current, and people in the Eastern Hemisphere can face a small radio and listen to the sound waves broadcast from the Western Hemisphere. Movies are mysterious enough, but now, in addition to moving, they are playing a sound. The power of the motor is enough, and in this century, perhaps we can see robots that don't use motors and electricity, universally replacing the power of motors and manpower. These are not uncommon. It is said that recently, some people have been able to move the cornea of ​​a blind person into the eye of another blind person, restoring the latter's visual function. There is also a scientist who has successfully tested the control of the formation of male and female fetuses. These are all things that people have dreamed of for thousands of years, and no one dared to believe that they would be realized one day, but now, the old man of science has shown them to us one by one. How can we not admit that science itself is a mystery that is more difficult to break than everything in nature?

We don't have to worry about how mysterious this mystery is. In short, science has made great and immeasurable contributions to mankind, and has made great and indescribable achievements to the culture of the world, which no one can deny. But if we turn around and take a look, my God, the face of this old man of science is completely different. The old man of science we see is working hard to use airplanes and cannons to desperately kill humans and destroy culture. Recently, I heard that some people are planning to use radio to control submarines and extract a large amount of chlorine gas from salt. Therefore, people can generally imagine the situation of the future world war, and how this old man of science will work hard to kill humans and destroy culture in the future world war.

Are the past achievements of the old man of science worthy of praise? Are the future sins worthy of cursing? This is a difficult question to answer, because it is science that creates prosperity, and it is also science that creates economic panic.

Science is really a mysterious to the extreme mystery, beyond all the mysteries of the natural world.

Playing Kingdoms

— Meng Tao

Tonight, I'm playing "Playing Kingdoms" with my nephew. What is "Playing Kingdoms"? It's about creating a small world on a small square slate. Because it's a small world, it's full of turmoil and uncertainty.

War is inevitable: the opportunity for war is getting closer and closer.

When the whole board is covered with different colors; I became a great power in one corner; my country's name is replaced by China, and I proudly added "Great".

My nephew's situation has been mostly surrounded by me; if I only decide to fight again; then maybe it will be my world of the blue sky, white sun, and red earth.

"Don't be afraid, I am Xiaojieshi; so I am Japan. The current Japan is me." My nephew said stubbornly.

Perhaps China is always a big country; so things are done carelessly. In a moment of carelessness, I lost the punch.

The end result is that Japan should beat China.

So in a corner of the earth, enemy iron hooves are all over the place; a small circle is drawn in a corner of China, which is regarded as the target of the war.

It was really unexpected. Every time he drew a circle, my nephew couldn't hit the target. This time, I watched him draw casually, and the old China was lost in confusion.

In the midst of roaring laughter, I vaguely heard: "Ha! Ha!...The old China, that's how it is!"

Offering Wine to Mr. Jin Songcen

— Chen Zhuzun

I have a bottle of wine. Washing away Lord Su's thousand years of sorrow. His writings can move heaven and earth. But his refined spirit cannot be sullied by vulgarity. How can books avoid being burned by emperors? The people are all like Chu prisoners. We are responsible for the rise and fall of the nation. Poetry is no different from the Spring and Autumn Annals. (Mr. Songcen is skilled in poetry, and his works are mostly related to poetic history. Recently, he revised the general history and wrote many biographies).

When you compose Parisian verses again in the future. Will you still have the same heroic feelings as before? (Douyin visited Paris last time and composed several quatrains. His heroic spirit and unrestrained interest made people clap their hands when they read them. Northeast Four Company Commanders

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-fourth: Drinking and Feasting, Crazy Merrymaking, and Containing Farewell Tears, Picking Lamps, Warming Dreams, and Singing Lowly Through the Long Night

After a while, he used a wooden tray to bring in two bowls of hot noodles and smiled at Ziqiang: Look how quickly I prepared them? Ziqiang said: It's quick, but I feel sorry for you staying up all night. Guizhi put down the tray, held the noodle bowl in both hands, respectfully, and put it in front of Ziqiang, and smiled: Even if it's tiring, it's only... the six words "just today for one night" were immediately swallowed, and then he said: If I could be so tired every night, I would be willing to. Ziqiang didn't want to ask further, so he picked up the bowl and ate the noodles. Guizhi didn't sit next to him and watch, but hummed and sang. Ziqiang picked up the noodles and looked at him and said: Why don't you eat some? Guizhi smiled: I'm happy to sing, I just want to keep singing, I won't be happy if I don't finish singing, I won't eat anything. Ziqiang thought he was telling the truth, so he didn't suspect anything. But at this time, the night was quiet, all the sounds had stopped, and any sound in the distance could naturally be heard clearly. Although Guizhi was sitting next to him, singing softly, the sound of the watchman's gong and clapper blown by the wind in the sky was still clear. Ziqiang understood that Guizhi didn't like to sing, but was afraid that he would hear the sound of the watchman's gong, which would not calm his mind, so he sang to distract him and cover up the sound of the watchman's gong. Looking at it this way, he was really well-intentioned. So he ignored the sound of the watchman's gong and listened to Guizhi's singing with his head shaking. After eating a bowl of noodles, he simply started singing himself, letting Guizhi eat the noodles. After singing a while of old songs, and then singing a while of Hua, he finally sang a passage of Qingyi in the Colored Building Match. Although the tune was out of tune and the taste was tasteless, he sang very happily. Guizhi thought that he had aroused Ziqiang's addiction to opera, so he sang loudly. He touched the teapot with his hand, the tea was cold, and he smiled: You eat noodles and then sing, it's salty and thirsty, I'll find some boiling water to make tea for you to drink. (321)

The Baby's One-Month Celebration

— Tang Zenggeng

I really can't bear to see my wife, who has suffered with me, pregnant for a full ten months. The sad, frowning, sallow face is still deeply in my mind. I also feel deeply uneasy and guilty about the trembling and pain during childbirth. Fortunately, the little life came to this world safely from birth, and now it has been a full month.

The baby's one-month celebration, Mom is happy, my wife is happy, and I am also happy, but because of the extreme financial difficulties recently, I don't want to have an unexpected expense for the one-month celebration, but for the sake of appearances, I have to reluctantly do it. Alas, for this false appearance, I really suffer for a lifetime.

"Today is Bao Bao's one-month celebration. No matter what, we have to find a way to do it. Besides, this is our first child," my wife said to me.

"Do it, how can I not want to do it? How can I not want to maintain appearances? But, without that damn money, what can I do?" I said with my head down, my face full of sadness and frustration.

My wife didn't say anything, and after a while, she said: "I still have two cotton-padded jackets here. You can pawn them first to get through this."

Thinking of this cold winter day, pawning my wife's only two cotton-padded jackets, I really feel a little uneasy, but my own have already been pawned, so I can only harden my heart and bite the bullet, carrying these two things, and under the snobbish eyes of the pawnshop owner, I exchanged them for two one-yuan bills.

With extreme displeasure, Mom and I bought some noodles, meat, and vegetables. It was for the one-month celebration of this first child. Although my face was full of forced smiles, my heart was extremely uncomfortable and sad.

We were busy all day, distributing the baby's one-month noodles to the neighbors, and we also invited several neighbors who lived together to have lunch together.

Meaningless, bland, we finally got through this baby's one-month celebration. I didn't feel any joy or pleasure, but only a painful scar was carved in the depths of my heart!

"Ah Gen's mother, oh my, I have never seen such a family. What one-month celebration for the first child, they did it so calmly. The one-month noodles were so bland and tasteless, and the meat was such a thin slice. When our Ah Mao had his one-month celebration, it was really more lively than them!"

"Yes, I have lived for forty years, and this is the first time I have seen such a one-month celebration. Except for this simple meal, there was no excitement at all. To be honest, my usual dishes are better than theirs. Hmph, we were unlucky to see such an unlucky family."

In the quiet of the night, I heard the landlady and the sister-in-law in the front building whispering. I could only smile bitterly at my wife sadly. My wife could only shed tears. Alas, the baby's one-month celebration, the false appearances; this snobbish world!

New Invention

Proof of Kerosene Curing Lung Disease (Part 1)

— Bingyu

On the 6th of this month, after I published my new invention of kerosene can cure lung disease in this column, I continuously received letters from Mr. Gao Yun, Bai Ou, Hong Ding, Wu Xieping, Gu Qian, Zhu Xinming, Zhang Guiheng, Wang Tongyi, and Wang Yi inquiring. The questions in the letters are roughly: (1) Requesting me to declare and disclose in detail to avoid patients from trying and harming lives? (2) Two or three out of ten compatriots nationwide suffer from pulmonary tuberculosis. If it is effective, it can save millions of lives? (3) Is the so-called kerosene the Asia brand, or the Mobil, Shell, and Monk Hat brands? (4) The number and time of drinking are still unclear? (5) What kind of side effects will occur after drinking, and will there be any danger? (6) Is this new invention hearsay? (7) The difference between kerosene and gasoline, etc. In order to prove and answer, I will translate in detail the thesis published by the special correspondent of the Japanese magazine "Housewife's Friend, Family Life Happiness Issue, New Year's Issue, and the facts proved by various medical doctors." (Please check the original text of the magazine from page 348 to page 365, entitled "Experimental Record of Curing Lung Disease with Kerosene" and the March issue of Housewife's Friend (236丨251) and "Kerosene Therapy for Tuberculosis" by Dr. Yamada Jushouichi, etc., but because this column is limited in space, it cannot be fully published after all, so I have to excerpt the main points and translate them to you. (1) Dr. Hayami Torazo, director of the Hyogo Prefectural Children's Research Institute, proved the results of the kerosene treatment for lung disease, which is 100% effective for 100 people. He said: Among hundreds of experimental subjects, only one had bad results. Why? Kerosene is originally an emulsion with strong bactericidal properties, and drinking it is harmless. I have been thinking about all kinds of facts and found it to be a very powerful discovery. The Russians and Eskimos have used kerosene as a substitute for wine since ancient times. A certain capitalist in Okayama Prefecture became healthy after drinking kerosene and later lived to be over 110 years old. None of the staff and workers in the Matsushita Kerosene Company in Yamaguchi Prefecture who work in the kerosene factory suffer from lung disease, but those who work in the office suffer from lung disease more often. After hearing these words, I hurriedly tried it on myself to check whether there were any harmful effects after drinking kerosene. However, although I did not suffer from lung disease, I coughed too much from smoking, so I drank kerosene 30 grams in several times, and as a result, my stomach and intestinal diseases and kidney diseases were completely cured. The most obvious phenomenon on the second day after I drank kerosene was increased appetite and sudden cessation of coughing. Afterwards, in order to check the bactericidal power of kerosene, I put tuberculosis bacteria in a culture dish and dropped a drop of diluted kerosene into the dish. The tuberculosis bacteria in the dish died without a trace. Now I am continuing to experiment with stone rats and rabbits, and the results have been published at the academic conference. After the experimental results, I am more convinced that it is safe and effective, so I advise people with lung disease to drink kerosene quickly. Now I will cite one or two cured examples to prove it. Mr. A, an assistant at a certain school, 27 years old, had both lungs ulcerated like honeycombs. In the past five or six years, he tried all treatment methods, and the condition went back and forth, and he could not be cured. Afterwards, he drank kerosene, 15 to 20 grams each time, and drank it six times in a week, and the lung disease was completely cured. Mr. K, a 22-year-old business student, was diagnosed with lung tip catarrh by the school doctor and a certain doctor. The inflammation disappeared immediately after drinking kerosene twice. Also, a friend of mine who suffered from spinal caries was also cured by drinking kerosene. We have a person working in the research institute who suffered from diabetes and was also cured with kerosene. In general, hundreds of people have asked me about drinking methods and have achieved good results. The effect has been as high as 100%. The method of drinking is slightly increased or decreased according to age and physique. But generally speaking, I drink 10 grams at first, and at most 15 grams. Gradually increase the amount from 10 grams. It is better to drink more times (one cup of kerosene is about 200 grams. It is best to buy a glass with grams engraved on it, so you won't have too much or too little.) The best time to drink is 9 pm. Stop dinner and drink before going to bed. Drink the second time after four to five days. Drink the third time after five days to a week. It is not difficult to drink, because you don't eat dinner, so you can avoid vomiting.

New Interpretation and Criticism of Old Medicine (Continued)

— Wang Qizhang

(5) Now let's discuss the old theory again. The Su Wen states that "if menstruation does not come, it is because the uterine pulse is closed. The uterine pulse belongs to the heart and is connected to the uterus. Now the qi is forced upwards to the lungs, and the heart qi cannot descend, so menstruation does not come." In general, heart qi descends and becomes blood. In women, it reaches the chest and descends, which is menstruation. If the qi is forced upwards to the lungs, then the true qi flows upwards, causing bitter mouth, dry tongue, and severe coughing when frightened. Expanding on this, blood comes from the heart and flows downwards, reaching the reproductive organs and becoming menstruation. This is a physiological phenomenon. If the qi is forced upwards to the lungs, then the blood flow is reversed, causing various symptoms. As for severe coughing, it is undoubtedly pulmonary tuberculosis that causes menstruation not to come. However, it is never mentioned that the disease is in the local part of the reproductive organs. The Golden Chamber also states that "because of deficiency and accumulation of cold, qi accumulates as a symptom, menstruation is cut off, and there is even prolonged cold blood accumulation in the uterine gate. Cold injures the meridians, and the coagulation is firm in the upper part, causing vomiting and saliva. Over time, it becomes lung carbuncle, and the body is damaged." In the end, accumulation of cold blood is the root cause, and over time, it becomes lung carbuncle. Lung carbuncle refers to the softening and rotting of lung tissue. This is already the late stage of pulmonary tuberculosis. This is another clear proof that menstruation is related to pulmonary tuberculosis. Zhang Congzheng said, "If menstruation does not come, do not take drastic hot medicines. If you take them, it will turn into lung consumption, bone steaming, tidal fever, coughing, pus, vomiting, and panting. The urine is astringent and stagnant, and sweating does not stop. Gradually, the body becomes thin and the pulse becomes large." These are all signs of late-stage pulmonary tuberculosis. Menstruation does not come because the body has already harbored tuberculosis. It is by no means caused by drastic hot medicines. Therefore, Li Qian said that if menstruation is not flowing, it is due to the four symptoms of deficiency, heat, fatigue, and qi not being regulated. Although these four symptoms have a very broad meaning, they are closely related to pulmonary tuberculosis. Deficiency means weakness. Heat means tidal fever. Fatigue means coughing up fatigue. Qi means difficulty breathing. It is not unreasonable to say that these four symptoms are caused by pulmonary tuberculosis. Wang Kentang's Zhizheng Zhunsheng states that "if a woman's menstruation is stopped, one of the three symptoms is that the spleen and stomach are damaged, food and drink are reduced, qi is consumed and blood is exhausted, and menstruation does not flow. The method should be to tonify the spleen and stomach, nourish the blood and qi, and wait for the qi to be sufficient and the blood to be produced, and the menstruation will flow by itself. Do not recklessly use menstruation-promoting agents, otherwise the central qi will be further damaged, and the yin blood will be further dried up, leading to consumptive diseases that cannot be saved." This clearly indicates that amenorrhea is caused by tuberculosis. Zhang Jiebin said, "If menstruation is gradually reduced and then stopped, and the hands, feet, bones, and flesh are painful, and the body gradually becomes thin, and tidal fever gradually develops, and the pulse is rapid, this is due to yin deficiency and blood weakness, and yang is rising. A small amount of water cannot extinguish the raging fire, and the fire forces the water to dry up, consuming body fluids." These are all signs of pulmonary tuberculosis. Kou Zongshi said, "If a woman is worried and thoughtful, she will injure her heart, and the blood will flow backwards and she will be thirsty. Her spirit will dissipate first, and her menstruation will stop first. Moreover, if she has heart disease, she will not be able to nourish the spleen, so she will not like to eat. If the spleen is deficient, then the metal will be deficient, so she will cough. If the kidney water is cut off, then the wood qi will not flourish, and the four limbs will be dry and withered, so she will be angry, her temples will be scorched, her muscles and bones will be withered. If the five organs spread, then she will die." Although these are all tuberculosis symptoms, there is no sign of uterine tuberculosis. Only pulmonary tuberculosis cannot be avoided. Therefore, Zhang Jingyue believed that there are different types of amenorrhea: blood obstruction and blood exhaustion. Obstruction is a temporary disease that can be cured by clearing it. Exhaustion comes on gradually and can be nourished by tonifying. Therefore, blood exhaustion cannot be treated by promoting menstruation. The so-called dry blood consumption belongs to blood exhaustion, and the principle is very clear. However, the cause of blood exhaustion must have its origin. The Abdominal Theory states that chest and hypochondriac fullness hinders eating, liver disease spreads to the spleen, and the patient hates the smell of blood and meat and clear liquid flows out. If the liver disease is accompanied by the lungs, then the patient will cough up blood. Hejian Six Books believes that young people who get drunk and enter the bedroom will exhaust their qi and injure their liver. If the liver is injured, the blood will dry up, and the spleen and stomach will transmit the disease, greatly depleting their blood, causing dizziness and irritability. Li Gao's Ten Books believes that blood and pulse fluids are transformed. Middle digestion causes stomach heat, and the patient eats well but gradually becomes thin, and fluids are not produced, so the muscles become thin and there is occasional thirst. The sea of blood is exhausted. The Introduction to Medicine states that after menstruation stops, excessive exertion, excessive intercourse, and eating dry and hot foods will cause fire to move, evil qi to flourish, and essence and blood to decline. Dongyuan also divides it into three causes: upper, middle, and lower. If the fire is in the upper part, it is caused by mental exertion. If the fire is in the middle part, the patient is prone to hunger and thirst. If the fire is in the lower part, the patient has constipation. In general, the cause of blood dryness is not limited to one factor. However, the so-called dry blood consumption originates from tuberculosis and belongs to blood exhaustion, so the cause of blood exhaustion should be the consumption of tuberculosis toxins, which affects the whole body, causing the eggs to not mature, and eventually menstruation does not come. It is definitely not caused by the local invasion of the congested and menstruating uterine lining by tuberculosis bacteria, causing anemia and interruption.

Based on all these factors and facts, Mr. Ding's so-called dry blood consumption is uterine tuberculosis, and he must have some basis for it. Otherwise, it is all speculation and not the truth. As far as I know, combined with the new theory and compared with the old theory, none of them match. It is difficult to accept. Is this a one-sided view of the new interpretation of old medicine? I ask Mr. Ding, what do you think?

The Treatment and Prevention of Tetanus

— Zhai Shaoheng

Umbilical tetanus is also known as tetanus. In my hometown, it is commonly called "locked jaw spasm," because when the disease occurs, the jaws become tightly closed, making breastfeeding impossible, hence the name. Regarding the cause of this disease, records from Hippocrates in ancient Greece, Europe, already identified its infectious nature. In 1884, Italians Galla and Rattone injected tissue fluid from around the abscesses of tetanus patients into rabbits, resulting in the same symptoms. The following year, Nicolaier and Rosenbach successively proved the spores and bacteria of this disease. Subsequently, Kitasato of Japan definitively determined the nature of the pathogen and the pure culture of the bacteria, making it clear that tetanus is caused by infection with tetanus bacteria. Today, in our country, still shrouded in mystery, except for a very small number of new doctors, people still hold absurd and unfounded beliefs. Superstitious people in my hometown believe that it is caused by someone opening or closing a lock in the room during childbirth. Therefore, before childbirth, all locks on boxes and drawers in the delivery room are usually opened to avoid the need to open locks when retrieving items during or after childbirth, believing this to be the only way to prevent the disease in the newborn. Therefore, those not opened before childbirth will not be opened within a certain period, even if necessary. If it is necessary to reopen what has already been opened, it is never locked again. Old doctors say that it is caused by wind entering the residual part of the umbilical cord after childbirth, so the umbilical area must be tightly wrapped. Considering that wind is generated by the flow of air, from the perspective of scientific medical bacteriology, this is not without a basis for misinterpretation. After all, the air contains countless kinds of bacteria. The purpose of wrapping is to avoid the entry of pathogenic bacteria. The so-called umbilical tetanus is actually caused by infection with what new medicine calls tetanus bacteria. Tetanus bacteria are a type of bacillus with one end enlarged, shaped like a mallet. They are extremely small and invisible to the naked eye. However, they can be clearly seen under a microscope. This bacteria primarily affects animals such as horses, cattle, sheep, pigs, and dogs. In countries with advanced medicine, it is now rare or nonexistent in humans. However, in our country, it is still seen from time to time, especially in newborns and infants. Once infected with this disease, it is almost certain death. Often, several children in a family die from this disease in succession, yet people still do not know the reason, which is truly pitiful.

This disease is always transmitted through wounds, so it is a wound-transmitted disease. If there is a wound on any part of our body, it can be invaded and cause this disease. It is not limited to the umbilical area of newborns. There is facial tetanus, caused by the entry of the bacteria through a wound on the face. There is puerperal tetanus, caused by the entry of the bacteria through a wound in the reproductive organs of a postpartum woman. Newborn tetanus is mostly caused by entry through the cut surface of the umbilical cord. Farmers are also sometimes affected, because tetanus bacteria thrive in the soil of fields and gardens. Traditional Chinese midwives often use broken pieces of bowls and tiles found on the ground as sharp instruments to cut the umbilical cord. If the bacteria are attached to these pieces, it is essentially directly planting tetanus into the umbilical area. Furthermore, the thread used to tie the umbilical cord and the cloth used to wrap it are invariably unclean. This is due to the ignorance of the midwives, leading to the transmission of this disease, resulting in the dire consequence of family extinction. It can be said that this is self-inflicted.

Now that the origin of this disease has been clarified, I will proceed to discuss the symptoms, prevention, and treatment of this disease.

Symptoms

The incubation period for tetanus is four to ten days, and sometimes more than three weeks. During the incubation period, there are absolutely no symptoms. Therefore, minor wounds are often healed during the longer incubation period, without knowing that the bacteria have already entered the body and are spreading. The initial signs are that the patient first feels stiffness and tension in the muscles of the lower jaw, face, and neck. Subsequently, due to facial muscle tension, a peculiar facial expression develops. The forehead is wrinkled, the nasolabial folds are deep, and the mouth is pulled to the left and right. It is difficult to open the mouth, and the jaws are tightly closed. The facial expression changes so much that even the patient's own mother often cannot recognize them. Neck stiffness varies in degree. Some people’s heads bend backwards, while others can still move freely. As the stiffness progresses, it gradually affects the muscles of the abdomen and back, and then the limbs and trunk. The body is stretched out stiff like a dried fish. This is called opisthotonos. The muscles of the back and the muscles of the upper and lower limbs undergo sustained tonic spasms, causing the body to arch backwards in a bow shape, which is called arcus spinalis. The degree of tension is constantly increased by impulse-like attacks. These attacks are often triggered by slight stimuli. Frequent attacks are accompanied by severe pain. Moreover, because the patient's consciousness remains perfectly clear and their senses are not impaired, the distress they exhibit is truly deserving of sympathy. At this time, the secretion of sweat glands and tear glands increases, causing tears and mucus to flow due to pain, which is enough to make onlookers feel sorrowful. Body temperature rises, reaching as high as 40 to 44 degrees Celsius. Breathing and swallowing are difficult due to spasms in the chest muscles and diaphragm. Heart function is also accelerated, and the pulse rate increases to 100 to 120. With prolonged fever, there is slight protein in the urine. If the muscles of the urethra and large intestine spasm, urination and defecation become difficult.

Prevention

The only way to prevent tetanus in newborns is to strictly disinfect the scissors, suture thread, umbilical cord bandage, and the hands of the midwife used to treat the umbilical cord. When the umbilical cord first falls off, the newly formed granulation tissue is essentially a wound and a very good opportunity for tetanus bacteria to invade. Therefore, attention should be paid to this. The only way to prevent tetanus in postpartum women is to emphasize disinfection. For other unclean wounds and wounds with difficult-to-remove foreign objects that are suspected of tetanus infection, in addition to implementing the local treatment described below, injecting 20 units of antitoxin around the wound every day for eight consecutive days as a preventive measure is beneficial and harmless. Do not hesitate. It is a pity that the effectiveness of preventive serum is not as significant in humans as it is in animals.

Treatment

There is no specific treatment for this disease. Even in countries with advanced medicine, the mortality rate is still between 50% and 90%. In China, it can be called an incurable disease. Therefore, the most important thing is to pay attention to prevention. I will now describe the general outline of currently popular treatments for the reference of those who unfortunately become infected. However, because the treatment is complex and the symptoms are constantly changing, it is more convenient to treat in a hospital.

Tetanus treatment is divided into general, local, serum, and drug therapy. These are described separately below.

(1) General Therapy: The patient should be moved to a quiet room to avoid excessive stimulation from sounds and sunlight, so as to avoid the hyperactivity of the reflex mechanism. Nutritious food should be provided, paying close attention to nutrition. For those with jaw tightness or difficulty swallowing, nutritious enemas should be used. (To be continued)

Q&A on Common Diseases

— Cheng Hanzhang

(25) Croupous Pneumonia

(Q) What is croupous pneumonia?

(A) It is a type of pneumonia caused by Streptococcus pneumoniae, affecting one lobe of the lung. Therefore, it is also called lobar pneumonia.

(Q) In what season is this disease most likely to occur?

(A) This disease occurs most often in winter and spring.

(Q) How is it spread?

(A) It is mostly transmitted directly from patients to healthy people.

(Q) What are the symptoms of a patient with croupous pneumonia?

(A) The patient suddenly begins with chills and shivering, accompanied by fever. This fever is generally persistent.

(Q) How high does the fever usually rise?

(A) It is between 39 and 41 degrees Celsius, which is approximately equivalent to 102 to 106 degrees Fahrenheit.

(Q) What does the patient feel?

(A) The patient feels very sick and complains of headache, fatigue, thirst, vomiting, etc.

(Q) What other symptoms are there?

(A) Stabbing pain in the chest, rapid breathing, rapid pulse, and coughing also occur. In severe cases, there may be coma and delirium.

(Q) What is the state of the expectorated sputum?

(A) Starting from the second day of the illness, the patient expectorates rusty-colored, viscous sputum. Streptococcus pneumoniae can be proven in the sputum.

(Q) Are there any abnormalities in respiratory movement?

(A) The respiratory movement on the affected side is slower.

(Q) Are the digestive organs affected?

(A) Some patients have constipation, while others have diarrhea. Some even develop severe flatulence due to poisoning.

(Q) What changes occur in the urine?

(A) The urine is concentrated: containing some protein, but the salt content is reduced.

(Q) Are there any changes in the spleen and blood?

(A) The spleen is enlarged; the number of white blood cells in the blood increases, and the number of eosinophils decreases. The number of Streptococcus pneumoniae seen in culture is related to the disease.

(Q) What is the course of croupous pneumonia?

(A) Typical croupous pneumonia lasts about a week; after sweating, the body temperature drops rapidly, and then enters the recovery period; however, in some cases, the fever subsides gradually. If the fever persists, there must be complications present: attention must be paid. (To be continued)

Various Infant Rashes

— Hou Guangdi

In spring, childhood diseases such as measles and pox are most prevalent. Since the widespread practice of vaccination, smallpox has decreased daily. However, measles, rubella, scarlet fever, etc., are still common in densely populated cities. If the rash symptoms are not identified early, it can lead to errors in treatment or negligence in prevention. Therefore, I will briefly describe the various rashes in children below. I hope this will attract the attention of hygiene experts.

First, those belonging to the roseola group are solitary, small, round, red spots, sometimes transient. They disappear when pressed with a finger. There are six types:

(A) Typhoid rose spots: These are localized and fixed light red spots, appearing between the nipples and navel, usually in the second week of the illness, lasting only a few days. Sometimes they slightly resemble skin rash, reaching the size of a lentil, round and sparse. This indicates typhoid fever.

(B) Prodromal rose spots of various infectious diseases: These are transient and temporary, often preceding the onset of rash, such as chickenpox, post-vaccination rashes, meningitis, pneumonia, rheumatism, polyarthritis, sepsis, mumps, miliary tuberculosis, influenza, angina, pertussis, erysipelas, diphtheria, and other diseases.

(C) Toxic rose spots: Such as those caused by meat poisoning, sausage poisoning, etc.

(D) Rose spots caused by skin irritation: Such as wet compresses of medicinal solutions, etc.

(E) Sweat rash caused by sweat secretion: Usually in areas with excessive sweating.

(F) Rose spots of miliary tuberculosis on the skin surface.

Second, rashes resembling measles are irregular, less distinct spots. Initially, they are small spots that enlarge to the size of a lentil or larger. There are seven types:

(A) Measles (common name: "sha zi"): It starts with small, punctate vesicles, then becomes uneven small spots, densely arranged like stars, slightly raised or flat on the skin. Although there is a vesicular nodule in the center of the spot, it rarely forms a skin blister and may contain blood infiltration. This rash first appears on the forehead and then the face, spreading to the entire body within three days.

(B) Rubella (German measles): Resembles measles but without skin rash. It is slightly scaly, about the size of a lentil, slightly round, and rarely fuses together. Initially, there appears to be a small nodule in the center, which gradually disappears. Rashes on the mucous membranes (such as the mouth), fingertips, and soles of the feet are not seen. It often affects the limbs, mostly on the extensor surfaces. This rash disappears in just two or three days, and the body temperature does not rise.

(C) Infectious erythema: Occurs on the trunk.

(D) Rashes that accompany other infectious diseases: Such as diphtheria, chickenpox, and post-vaccination rashes, are often difficult to distinguish. Diagnosis relies on observation of other symptoms and the course of fever.

(E) Drug rashes: Such as those caused by antipyretics, green algae, ice, and serum injections. They often start with wheals (urticaria) accompanied by continuous fever and proteinuria. The rash often starts at the injection site, and symmetrical rashes appear on both limbs, spreading to the face.

(F) Atypical scarlet fever: The rash often clusters in several areas, interspersed with pale skin. It is more common on the body and less on the face, or even absent. The differences from measles are that it appears earlier and is accompanied by vomiting and angina.

(G) Atypical urticaria.

Third, rashes resembling scarlet fever are tiny, intensely red, dense spots appearing on a uniformly red background.

(A) Scarlet fever rash: Consists of tiny spots that initially appear separate and then merge with the red background to form a continuous sheet. Within hours, it spreads from the neck and chest to the face and body, and within 24 hours to the limbs. The triangle around the mouth is often spared, or the rash may be absent altogether. The rash on both cheeks completely merges together. There is significant high fever with slight itching and other associated symptoms.

(B) Fourth Disease (Dukes' Disease): Differs from scarlet fever in that the symptoms are mild, there is no mucosal involvement, and no other complications.

(C) Rashes of other infectious diseases: Such as typhoid fever, pneumonia, influenza, sepsis, diphtheria, and chickenpox. The difference from scarlet fever is the lack of red spots and the gradual merging of the surrounding red areas (before the onset of scarlet fever).

(D) Drug rashes and serum sickness: Such as those caused by ingestion of atropine, quinine, salicylic acid, opium, mercury, and injection of heterologous serum. The rash appears as early as the second day after injection or as late as twenty days, but mostly between the eighth and fourteenth days. It resembles scarlet fever, but the red color is slightly less intense and more diffuse. The affected area also resembles scarlet fever, but the intensity is reduced. It often starts at the injection site, causing nearby abscesses and proteinuria, and continuous fever. There is no vomiting or desquamation (unlike scarlet fever).

(E) Scarlet fever-like rashes in the convalescent stage of diphtheria: The rash resembles scarlet fever (and the serum rash mentioned above) even without injection. However, it is accompanied by tonsillitis and a positive Schick test. This syndrome is most likely a variant of scarlet fever that occurs after acquiring immunity to diphtheria.

Fourth, circular and arcuate erythema: Larger, raised red spots form a circle as the central area becomes less pigmented. They spread around the perimeter or merge with each other, or partially disappear, resulting in fantastic shapes.

(A) Polymorphous exudative erythema: Occurs on the outer aspects of the limbs and the backs of the hands and feet. It does not desquamate and is transient. It is often accompanied by fever, joint pain, edema, proteinuria, and other symptoms.

(B) Drug poisoning rashes: Such as those caused by quinine, salicylic acid, etc., and the injection of heterologous serum, are often associated with gastrointestinal disorders.

Fifth, syphilitic rashes are brownish-red or copper-colored round rashes that appear raised on the skin. There is no fixed exudate. These include macular syphilitic rashes, which can be seen on the palms and soles of the feet. They are faint and persistent, with a shimmering appearance, like a fresh slice. The outer edge is like a ring.

Tuberculosis Prevention Drug and its Inventor, Guerin (4)

(Translated by Havas News Agency from the October 14, 1933 issue of L'Illustration in Paris)

Moreover, the method of administration is the same for everyone. (Take three grams of B.C.G., divided into three doses, one gram per dose, taken within 24 hours, i.e., swallowed on an empty stomach half an hour before breakfast.) After three months, 82 people (i.e., 55%) had a reaction to the tuberculin test, thus becoming reactive. The proportion of people who become reactive is 10% higher than the proportion obtained from children who have received subcutaneous injections. At the time of publication of this article, the first bottled serum for oral administration to adults and two-year-old children has been delivered to the provinces.

The Fortress of Tuberculosis Prevention

All these organizations (laboratories, B.C.G. preparation, and animals and paper label cabinets used for testing) must be suitable for the great construction of the Pasteur Institute and France. For several months, the Tuberculosis Research Institute has been established in a three-story building, high on Falguiere Street, where the front door is located, and a five-story side stands above the garden of the Institute. The laboratories inside are the most beautiful in the world. Construction began three years ago, and was decided upon by Pasteur Institute Director Mr. Roux and the Institute's Board of Directors. The initial estimated cost was eight million, of which six million was allocated from the fund, and the remaining two million was provided by the state from horse racing taxes. In fact, the total cost of the project is close to ten million, because the building is based on simplicity and grandeur. The initial plans were made by architect Mr. Duquesne, but he died before the work was completed, so Mr. Bitterlin completed the work. Due to limited space, the writer cannot adequately describe this French scientific sanctuary, but in general, it can be divided into three parts: one part for the manufacture of B.C.G., one part for the chemical examination, and one part for the experimental animals and various attachments. The founders adhered to a principle of separating the department for manufacturing preventive drugs from the chemical examination department for culturing virulent bacteria. On the first floor facing Falgniere Street, under the direct supervision of Dr. Guerin, experts prepare materials for culturing B.C.G. vaccine, or engage in planting affairs, or emulsification of the original preventive medicine. The method uses a rotating electric device with rust-proof small steel balls to achieve this. After that, the medicine is poured into small bottles with a dispensing device, and the bottle mouth is sealed with fire. The scene on the second floor of the building seems the most miscellaneous. There is a large laboratory for practical work, which can accommodate 24 people working at the same time, studying various types of tuberculosis in humans or animals. In addition, there are laboratories for various directors, and the most peculiar laboratory, which can be called the "bacterial kitchen", which specializes in preparing the materials required for microorganisms and should be planted on them (i.e., potato, beef bile, etc.). In addition, the most interesting thing is the collection of various strains, each of which is labeled with an explanation of its history. There is a large cabinet divided into three compartments, which contains as many as 600 strains (from human strains to various strains of cattle, birds, and decaying grass). The style is the same, but the functions are different. If each compartment stores about 1,200 tubes, and each tube contains countless microorganisms (even if you use the number of 300 million or 400 million to describe it, you cannot describe its multitude), when we look at the door of this strain cabinet, we cannot help but feel reverence. Now we will not stay temporarily in the ten constant temperature rooms and the chemotherapy laboratories built on the roof, etc., but quickly visit the animal breeding farm. There are as many as 8,000 small animals there, all raised in two large rooms upstairs and downstairs, in lead-skinned boxes with iron steel, and each box has a number and activity beam label (written with the names of guinea pigs, rabbits, rats, etc.). Sheep and goats, etc., are kept in other rooms. In addition, there is a place for raising monkeys, with a total of 200 monkeys (this newspaper has talked about it for a long time five years ago), and there is a chicken farm near the roof, with 200 chickens. It is used for testing, just like guinea pigs. There are two dissecting rooms for the corpses of each dead or sacrificed animal. One is specially used for inspecting the animals that have received B.C.G., and the other is specially used for inspecting the animals that have been used for various tuberculosis research experiments. Now I have narrated to the end of the visit, and the main impressions I have gained are surprise and admiration. However, our French people sometimes like to belittle themselves, so they have also publicized the rudeness of our country's chemical examination rooms, even counting the number of broken windows, broken tables, and decayed equipment. May I ask if we are close to the truth? In fact, there has been great progress in various parts of France in recent years, such as the nursery school of the Medical College of the University of Paris, the new chemical examinations of the French Academy of Sciences, and the major sanatoriums in Bligny, Ainccurt, and Helfaut, etc. Today, French scientists are no longer the shabby figures in myths, and the equipment they need has also been manufactured exquisitely. The most important thing to do now is to promote and apply the inventions of these scientists, because there are still many doctors and people who still have the old concept of B.C.G. ten years ago. How can we know that preventive injections are limited to children in sick families? This is a thing of the past. Now all French people, especially children who have reached the age of schooling (as long as they meet the conditions for receiving seedlings), should enjoy this invention. Since the great era of Pasteur, this can be undoubtedly called the most miraculous invention. (The End)

Scheduled to be held at Tianjin Institute of Technology on March 24th
